            local farmId = farm:GetAttribute("farmId") or farm.Name
            safeServiceCall(FarmService, "claim", farmId)
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
        return
    end
    for _, farmName in ipairs(selected) do
        local farmId = farmIdMap[farmName]
        if farmId then
            safeServiceCall(FarmService, "claim", farmId)
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end
end
function getAncientMerchantOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local merchantList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "AncientMerchant" }, "AncientMerchant") or {}
    for i, offer in ipairs(merchantList) do
        local name = offer.item and offer.item.nm or "Unknown"
        local amount = offer.item and offer.item.am or 1
        local price = offer.price or 0
        local display = (amount > 1 and (amount .. "x " .. name) or name) .. " - " .. tostring(price) .. " tickets"
        table.insert(options, display)
        map[display] = { name = name, amount = amount, price = price, index = i }
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end
function autoBuyAncientMerchantStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedAncientMerchantItems"])
    if #selected == 0 then return end
    local _, itemMap = getAncientMerchantOptions()
    local merchantList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "AncientMerchant" }, "AncientMerchant") or {}
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local bought = data.ancientMerchantBought or {}
    local slots = Values and Values.ancientMerchantSlots and Values.ancientMerchantSlots(client, data) or 3
    local serverTime = getServerTimeNowSafe()
    for slot = 1, slots do
        local ts = DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(serverTime + 3600):ToUniversalTime()
        local seed = ts.Year * 222 + ts.Month * 333 + ts.Day * 444444 + ts.Hour * 33333 + client.UserId + slot
        local itemData = merchantList[Functions.getRandom and Functions.getRandom(merchantList, seed) or 1]
        if itemData and itemData.item then
            local merchantName = itemData.item.nm or ""
            local merchantAmount = itemData.item.am or 1
            for _, displayName in ipairs(selected) do
                local selectedItem = itemMap[displayName]
                if selectedItem and merchantName == selectedItem.name and merchantAmount == selectedItem.amount then
                    local key = string.format("%*", seed)
                    if not bought[key] then
                        safeServiceCall(RewardService, "buyAncientMerchant", slot)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function archiveUnwantedPetsStep()
    local numToKeep = tonumber(Library.Flags["PetsToKeepCount"]) or 20
    local keepEvent = Library.Flags["KeepEventPets"] ~= false
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.pet then return end
    local allPets = {}
    for petId, petRaw in pairs(data.inventory.pet) do
        local petObject = itemUtils.createItemFromData and itemUtils.createItemFromData(petRaw)
        if petObject then
            table.insert(allPets, { id = petId, name = petObject:getName(), multiplier = petObject:getMultiplier() })
        end
    end
    table.sort(allPets, function(a, b) return a.multiplier > b.multiplier end)
    local keepIds = {}
    for i = 1, math.min(numToKeep, #allPets) do keepIds[allPets[i].id] = true end
    if data.equippedPets then for petId in pairs(data.equippedPets) do keepIds[petId] = true end end
    for _, petData in ipairs(allPets) do
        local petDef = PetsModule[petData.name]
        if petDef then
            if petDef.special then keepIds[petData.id] = true end
            if petDef.specialMultiplier and keepEvent then keepIds[petData.id] = true end
        end
    end
    local archiveIds = {}
    for petId in pairs(data.inventory.pet) do if not keepIds[petId] then archiveIds[petId] = true end end
    if next(archiveIds) then safeServiceCall(PetService, "archivePets", archiveIds, 1) end
end
function claimExplorerHintsStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.explorerHints then return end
    if not data.explorerHints.hint1 then
        safeServiceCall(ExplorerService, "collectHint", 1)
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
    data = getData()
    if data and data.explorerHints and data.explorerHints.hint1 and not data.explorerHints.hint2 then
        safeServiceCall(ExplorerService, "collectHint", 2)
    end
end
function collectScatteredExplorerItemsStep()
    local room = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Game") and Workspace.Game:FindFirstChild("Maps") and Workspace.Game.Maps:FindFirstChild("Spaceship")
    room = room and room:FindFirstChild("extra explorer room")
    if not room then return end
    for _, item in ipairs(room:GetChildren()) do
        local prompt = item:FindFirstChildOfClass("ProximityPrompt")
        if prompt and fireproximityprompt then
            pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(prompt) end)
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end
end
function activateLightSwitchesStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local switchEvent = pcall(function()
        return ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Knit.Services:GetChildren()[20]:FindFirstChild("RE"):GetChildren()[4]
    end)
    if not switchEvent then return end
    for buildingId in pairs(BuildingsList) do
        if buildingId:lower():find("lightswitch") and data.buildings and data.buildings[buildingId] then
            local switchNumber = buildingId:match("lightSwitch(%d+)")
            if switchNumber then
                local switchId = tonumber(switchNumber)
                local activated = false
                if type(data.lightSwitches) == "table" then
                    for _, id in ipairs(data.lightSwitches) do
                        if id == switchId then activated = true break end
                    end
                end
                if not activated then
                    pcall(function() switchEvent:FireServer(switchId) end)
                    task.wait(0.25)
                    for _, map in pairs(Workspace:FindFirstChild("Game") and Workspace.Game:FindFirstChild("Maps") and Workspace.Game.Maps:GetChildren() or {}) do
                        local sw = map:FindFirstChild("LightSwitch" .. switchId) or map:FindFirstChild("lightSwitch" .. switchId) or map:FindFirstChild("Light Switch " .. switchId)
                        if sw then
                            local prompt = sw:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt", true)
                            if prompt and fireproximityprompt then pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(prompt) end) end
                            local cd = sw:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
                            if cd then pcall(function() fireclickdetector(cd) end) end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function autoEquipBestAxeStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.exclusive then return end
    local axeIndex = nil
    for inventoryIndex, itemData in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
        local ok, itemObj = pcall(function() return itemUtils.createItemFromData(itemData) end)
        if ok and itemObj then
            local ok2, itemName = pcall(function() return itemObj:getName():lower() end)
            if ok2 and itemName:find("axe") and not itemName:find("pickaxe") then
                axeIndex = inventoryIndex
                break
            end
        end
    end
    if not axeIndex or data.isAxeEquipped then return end
    local unequipIndex = nil
    if data.isPickaxeEquipped then
        for inventoryIndex, itemData in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
            local ok, itemObj = pcall(function() return itemUtils.createItemFromData(itemData) end)
            if ok and itemObj then
                local ok2, itemName = pcall(function() return itemObj:getName():lower() end)
                if ok2 and itemName:find("pickaxe") then
                    unequipIndex = inventoryIndex
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if not unequipIndex and data.isFishingRodEquipped then
        for inventoryIndex, itemData in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
            local ok, itemObj = pcall(function() return itemUtils.createItemFromData(itemData) end)
            if ok and itemObj then
                local ok2, itemName = pcall(function() return itemObj:getName():lower() end)
                if ok2 and (itemName:find("fishingrod") or itemName:find("rod")) then
                    unequipIndex = inventoryIndex
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if unequipIndex then
        safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", unequipIndex)
        task.wait(1)
    end
    safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", axeIndex)
end
function setTreeCooldownBypass(enabled)
    if not TreeController then return end
    if enabled then
        TreeController._debounce = setmetatable({}, {
            __index = function() return false end,
            __newindex = function() end,
        })
    else
        TreeController._debounce = {}
    end
end
function setAxeStrengthBypass(enabled)
    if not TreeController then return end
    if enabled then
        TreeController._RCUOriginalIsStrongEnough = TreeController._RCUOriginalIsStrongEnough or TreeController.isStrongEnough
        TreeController.isStrongEnough = function() return true end
    elseif TreeController._RCUOriginalIsStrongEnough then
        TreeController.isStrongEnough = TreeController._RCUOriginalIsStrongEnough
    end
end
function setHideAuraAnimations(enabled)
    if not AuraController then return end
    if enabled then
        AuraController._RCUOriginalPlayAura = AuraController._RCUOriginalPlayAura or AuraController.playAura
        AuraController.playAura = function() end
    elseif AuraController._RCUOriginalPlayAura then
        AuraController.playAura = AuraController._RCUOriginalPlayAura
    end
end
RCUBlackScreenGui, RCUBlackScreenActive = nil, false
function toggleBlackScreen(forceState)
    if forceState ~= nil then RCUBlackScreenActive = forceState else RCUBlackScreenActive = not RCUBlackScreenActive end
    if RCUBlackScreenActive then
        if not RCUBlackScreenGui then
            RCUBlackScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
            RCUBlackScreenGui.Name = "RCU_BlackScreen"
            RCUBlackScreenGui.DisplayOrder = 999999
            RCUBlackScreenGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
            RCUBlackScreenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
            RCUBlackScreenGui.Parent = client:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("PlayerGui") or Instance.new("Folder")
            local bg = Instance.new("Frame")
            bg.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            bg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
            bg.BorderSizePixel = 0
            bg.Parent = RCUBlackScreenGui
            local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
            label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 10)
            label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            label.Text = "Black screen active | F3 or Wake Up to exit"
            label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
            label.TextSize = 14
            label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            label.Parent = bg
            local wakeBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            wakeBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
            wakeBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -100, 0.5, -25)
            wakeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
            wakeBtn.Text = "Wake Up"
            wakeBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            wakeBtn.TextSize = 18
            wakeBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
            wakeBtn.Parent = bg
            wakeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() toggleBlackScreen(false) end)
        end
        RCUBlackScreenGui.Enabled = true
    elseif RCUBlackScreenGui then
        RCUBlackScreenGui.Enabled = false
    end
end
UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gpe)
    if gpe then return end
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F3 then toggleBlackScreen() end
end)
function disableParticleEffects(root)
    for _, obj in ipairs(root:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or obj:IsA("Trail") or obj:IsA("Beam") or obj:IsA("Fire") or obj:IsA("Smoke") or obj:IsA("Sparkles") then
            obj.Enabled = false
        end
    end
end
function stripTextures(root)
    for _, obj in ipairs(root:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("Texture") or obj:IsA("Decal") then obj.Transparency = 1 end
    end
end
function extractPrivateServerId(input)
    local code = tostring(input or "")
    return code:match("code=([%w]+)") or code
end
function rejoinPublicServer()
    local placeId = game.PlaceId
    local cursor = ""
    local url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"
    local servers = {}
    while true do
        local reqUrl = url .. (cursor ~= "" and ("&cursor=" .. cursor) or "")
        local ok, response = pcall(function() return HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet(reqUrl)) end)
        if not ok or not response or not response.data then break end
        for _, server in ipairs(response.data) do
            if server.playing < server.maxPlayers then table.insert(servers, server) end
        end
        if not response.nextPageCursor then break end
        cursor = response.nextPageCursor
    end
    table.sort(servers, function(a, b) return a.playing < b.playing end)
    for _, server in ipairs(servers) do
        if server.id ~= game.JobId then
            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, server.id, client)
            break
        end
    end
end
function rejoinPrivateServer()
    local accessCode = extractPrivateServerId(Library.Flags["PrivateServerId"])
    if accessCode == "" then return end
    local options = Instance.new("TeleportOptions")
    options.ReservedServerAccessCode = accessCode
    TeleportService:Teleport(game.PlaceId, client, options)
end
function claimAllBeedexBypass()
    local beedexRewards = BeedexRewards or {}
    local total = #beedexRewards
    if total == 0 then total = 20 end
    notify("Beedex Bypass", "Firing " .. total .. " reward claims...", "warning")
    local claimed = 0
    for i = 1, total do
        local ok = serviceCallSucceeded(safeServiceCall(HiveService, "claimBeedexReward", i))
        if ok then claimed = claimed + 1 end
        task.wait(0.2)
    end
    notify("Beedex Bypass", "Done. Fired " .. claimed .. "/" .. total .. " claims.", "info")
end
function updateHiveStatusLabel(labelObject)
    if not labelObject or not labelObject.Set then return end
    local data = getData()
    if not data then setVersusLabelText(labelObject, "Hive: loading...") return end
    local honey = 0
    local honeyItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, "honey")
    if honeyItem then honey = honeyItem:getAmount() end
    local toCollect = data.honeyToCollect or 0
    local equipped = 0
    if data.equippedBees then for _ in pairs(data.equippedBees) do equipped = equipped + 1 end end
    local text = string.format("Honey: %s | To collect: %s | Bees equipped: %d", tostring(honey), tostring(toCollect), equipped)
    setVersusLabelText(labelObject, text)
end
function startHiveStatusLabelUpdater(labelObject)
    task.spawn(function()
        while labelObject and labelObject.Parent do
            updateHiveStatusLabel(labelObject)
            task.wait(3)
        end
    end)
end

-- detailed status + feature helpers
RCUStatusLabels = RCUStatusLabels or {}
RCUSessionStats = RCUSessionStats or {
    StartedAt = os.time(),
    Hatches = 0,
    Rebirths = 0,
    TreesCut = 0,
    OresMined = 0,
    FishCaught = 0,
    DungeonsCleared = 0,
}
function incrementSessionStat(key, amount)
    amount = tonumber(amount) or 1
    RCUSessionStats[key] = (tonumber(RCUSessionStats[key]) or 0) + amount
end
function startVersusLabelUpdater(labelObject, tag, builder, intervalSeconds)
    if not labelObject then return end
    intervalSeconds = math.max(tonumber(intervalSeconds) or 3, 1)
    local tagName = tag or ("RCU_Label_" .. tostring(math.random(10000, 99999)))
    Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag(tagName)
    local lastText = ""
    local lastAt = 0
    local conn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        local now = os.clock()
        if now - lastAt < intervalSeconds then return end
        lastAt = now
        local ok, text = pcall(builder)
        if ok and text and text ~= lastText then
            lastText = text
            setVersusLabelText(labelObject, text)
        end
    end)
    Library:TrackConnection(conn, tagName)
    pcall(function() setVersusLabelText(labelObject, builder()) end)
end
function buildMainDashboardText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Dashboard: waiting for data..." end
    local lines = {
        "Clicks: " .. formatShortNumber(getCurrency(data, "clicks")),
        "Gems: " .. formatShortNumber(getCurrency(data, "gems")),
        "Rebirths: " .. formatShortNumber(data.rebirths or 0),
        "Pets: " .. tostring(countTable(data.pets or data.inventory and data.inventory.pet or {})),
        "Session: " .. getSessionDurationText(),
    }
    return table.concat(lines, " | ")
end
function buildRebirthInfoText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Rebirth: loading..." end
    local clicks = getCurrency(data, "clicks")
    local current = tonumber(data.rebirths) or 0
    local best = getBestRebirthIndex()
    local bestAmount = best > 0 and RebirthList[best] or 0
    local mode = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedRebirthAmount"], "Max Unlocked")
    return string.format("Rebirths: %s | Clicks: %s | Best: %s (%s) | Mode: %s", formatShortNumber(current), formatShortNumber(clicks), tostring(best), formatShortNumber(bestAmount), tostring(mode))
end
function getRebirthDropdownOptions()
    local options = { "Max Unlocked" }
    for index, amount in ipairs(RebirthList) do
        table.insert(options, formatShortNumber(amount) .. " Rebirths (#" .. tostring(index) .. ")")
    end
    return options
end
function resolveRebirthIndexFromFlag()
    local selected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedRebirthAmount"], "Max Unlocked")
    if selected == "Max Unlocked" or selected == "Best" then return getBestRebirthIndex() end
    local index = tonumber(tostring(selected):match("#(%d+)"))
    if index and RebirthList[index] then return index end
    return getBestRebirthIndex()
end
function getNormalUpgradeNames()
    local names = {}
    for upgradeId, info in pairs(upgradesList or {}) do
        local label = info.name or info.displayName or humanizeToken(upgradeId)
        table.insert(names, label)
        names[label] = upgradeId
    end
    table.sort(names)
    return names
end
function buySelectedUpgradesBatch(maxBuys)
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedNormalUpgrades"])
    if #selected == 0 then return buyNormalUpgradesBatch(maxBuys) end
    local nameToId = {}
    for upgradeId, info in pairs(upgradesList or {}) do
        local label = info.name or info.displayName or humanizeToken(upgradeId)
        nameToId[label] = upgradeId
    end
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return 0 end
    local bought = 0
    local gems = getCurrency(data, "gems")
    for _, label in ipairs(selected) do
        if bought >= (tonumber(maxBuys) or 5) then break end
        local upgradeId = nameToId[label]
        local upgradeInfo = upgradeId and upgradesList[upgradeId]
        local nextUpgrade = upgradeId and getNextNormalUpgrade(upgradeId, upgradeInfo, data)
        local cost = nextUpgrade and tonumber(nextUpgrade.cost)
        if cost and cost <= gems then
            local result = safeServiceCall(UpgradeService, "upgrade", upgradeId)
            if result == "success" or result == true then
                bought = bought + 1
                gems = math.max(0, gems - cost)
                task.wait(0.12)
                data = getData() or data
            end
        end
    end
    return bought
end
function getHatchAmountFromFlag()
    local selected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedHatchAmount"], "Max")
    if selected == "1x" then return 1 end
    if selected == "3x" then return 3 end
    return math.huge
end
function shouldUseLuckyEggs()
    return Library.Flags["UseLuckyEggs"] == true
end
function getPlayerPetCraftOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local data = getData()
    if not data or type(data.inventory) ~= "table" or type(data.inventory.pet) ~= "table" then return { "None" }, map end
    local counts = {}
    for petId, raw in pairs(data.inventory.pet) do
        local petObject = itemUtils.createItemFromData and itemUtils.createItemFromData(raw)
        if petObject then
            local name = petObject:getName()
            local tier = raw.tier or raw.t or "Normal"
            local display = name .. (tier ~= "" and tier ~= "Normal" and (" [" .. tier .. "]") or "")
            counts[display] = (counts[display] or 0) + 1
            map[display] = map[display] or {}
            table.insert(map[display], petId)
        end
    end
    for display, amount in pairs(counts) do
        table.insert(options, display .. " x" .. tostring(amount))
    end
    table.sort(options)
    if #options == 0 then table.insert(options, "None") end
    return options, map
end
function craftSelectedPetsStep(maxCrafts)
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedCraftPets"])
    if #selected == 0 then return end
    local _, map = getPlayerPetCraftOptions()
    maxCrafts = tonumber(maxCrafts) or 3
    local done = 0
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.pet then return end
    for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
        if done >= maxCrafts then break end
        local baseName = display:match("^(.-) x%d+$") or display
        local petIds = map[baseName] or map[display]
        if type(petIds) == "table" then
            for _, petId in ipairs(petIds) do
                local raw = data.inventory.pet[petId]
                local amt = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.am or 0) or 0
                if amt >= 5 then
                    local ok = pcall(function()
                        PetService:craft({ [1] = petId }, true, 1)
                    end)
                    if ok then
                        done = done + 1
                        task.wait(0.2)
                    end
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function craftSelectedPetsAmountOnce()
    local amount = math.max(tonumber(Library.Flags["PetCraftAmount"]) or 1, 1)
    for _ = 1, amount do
        craftSelectedPetsStep(1)
        task.wait(0.35)
    end
end
function getInventoryBoxOptions()
    local options = {}
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory then return { "All Boxes" } end
    local seen = {}
    for category, container in pairs(data.inventory) do
        if type(container) == "table" and (tostring(category):find("box") or tostring(category):find("crate")) then
            for _, raw in pairs(container) do
                local name = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.nm or raw.name) or tostring(raw)
                if name and not seen[name] then
                    seen[name] = true
                    table.insert(options, name)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    for name in pairs(PotionsList or {}) do
        if tostring(name):lower():find("box") or tostring(name):lower():find("crate") then addUnique(options, name) end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    table.insert(options, 1, "All Boxes")
    return options
end
function useSelectedBoxesStep(limit)
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedBoxTypes"])
    local useAll = #selected == 0 or selected[1] == "All Boxes"
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory then return end
    limit = tonumber(limit) or 15
    local used = 0
    for category, container in pairs(data.inventory) do
        if used >= limit then break end
        if type(container) == "table" then
            for itemId, raw in pairs(container) do
                if used >= limit then break end
                local name = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.nm or raw.name) or ""
                local isBox = tostring(name):lower():find("box") or tostring(name):lower():find("crate") or tostring(category):lower():find("box")
                if isBox and (useAll or hasValue(selected, name)) then
                    safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", itemId)
                    used = used + 1
                    task.wait(0.08)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function getPotionNameOptions()
    local options = {}
    for name in pairs(PotionsList or {}) do addUnique(options, name) end
    table.sort(options)
    if #options == 0 then table.insert(options, "All Potions") end
    table.insert(options, 1, "All Potions")
    return options
end
function useSelectedPotionsStep(limit)
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedPotionTypes"])
    local useAll = #selected == 0 or selected[1] == "All Potions"
    limit = tonumber(limit) or 10
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local used = 0
    local containers = { data.inventory and data.inventory.potion, data.inventory and data.inventory.potions }
    for _, container in ipairs(containers) do
        if type(container) == "table" then
            for itemId, raw in pairs(container) do
                if used >= limit then break end
                local name = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.nm or raw.name) or ""
                if useAll or hasValue(selected, name) then
                    safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", itemId)
                    used = used + 1
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function getGardenSeedTypeOptions()
    local options = {}
    for seedType in pairs(GardenSeeds or {}) do addUnique(options, seedType) end
    table.sort(options)
    return options
end
function autoPlantSelectedSeedTypesStep(maxPlants)
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedGardenSeedTypes"])
    if #selected == 0 then autoPlantGardenSeedsStep(maxPlants) return end
    maxPlants = tonumber(maxPlants) or 6
    local planted = 0
    for _, seedType in ipairs(selected) do
        for slotId in ipairs(getGardenSlotIds()) do
            if planted >= maxPlants then return end
            safeServiceCall(GardenService, "plant", slotId, seedType)
            planted = planted + 1
            task.wait(0.15)
        end
    end
end

function autoBuySelectedHiveUpgradesStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedHiveUpgrades"])
    local idByName = {}
    for upgradeId, info in pairs(HiveUpgrades or {}) do
        idByName[info.name or humanizeToken(upgradeId)] = upgradeId
    end
    if #selected == 0 then
        for upgradeId in pairs(HiveUpgrades or {}) do
            safeServiceCall(HiveService, "buyHiveUpgrade", upgradeId)
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
        return
    end
    for _, label in ipairs(selected) do
        local upgradeId = idByName[label]
        if upgradeId then
            safeServiceCall(HiveService, "buyHiveUpgrade", upgradeId)
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end
end

function getAuraDiceDisplayOptions()

    for id, info in pairs(auraDices) do

function rollSelectedAuraDiceStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedAuraDiceRoll"])
    local options, map = getAuraDiceDisplayOptions()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    if #selected == 0 then safeServiceCall(AuraService, "roll") return end
    local pool = {}
    for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
        local id = map[display]
        if id then
            local item = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, id)
            if item and item:getAmount() > 0 then table.insert(pool, id) end
        end
    end
    if #pool > 0 then safeServiceCall(AuraService, "roll", pool[math.random(#pool)]) end
end
function getAuraDiceCraftDisplayOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local recipes = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "AuraDiceCrafting" }, "AuraDiceCrafting") or {}
    for index, recipe in ipairs(recipes) do
        if recipe.item and recipe.reward then
            local display = recipe.item:getName() .. " -> " .. recipe.reward:getName()
            table.insert(options, display)
            map[display] = index
        end
    end
    return options, map
end
function craftSelectedAuraDiceStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedAuraDiceCraft"])
    local _, map = getAuraDiceCraftDisplayOptions()
    local recipes = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "AuraDiceCrafting" }, "AuraDiceCrafting") or {}
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local targets = selected
    if #targets == 0 then for display in pairs(map) do table.insert(targets, display) end end
    for _, display in ipairs(targets) do
        local recipeIndex = map[display]
        local recipe = recipeIndex and recipes[recipeIndex]
        if recipe and recipe.item then
            local requiredName = recipe.item:getName()
            local requiredAmount = recipe.item:getAmount()
            local playerItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, requiredName)
            local playerAmount = playerItem and playerItem:getAmount() or 0
            local maxCraftable = math.floor(playerAmount / math.max(requiredAmount, 1))
            if maxCraftable > 0 then
                safeServiceCall(AuraService, "craftDice", recipeIndex, maxCraftable)
                task.wait(0.35)
            end
        end
    end
end
function buildAxeUpgradeStatusText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.exclusive then return "Axe: no data" end
    local currentName, currentIndex = "None", 0
    for _, raw in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
        local item = itemUtils.createItemFromData and itemUtils.createItemFromData(raw)
        if item then
            local name = item:getName():lower()
            if name:find("axe") and not name:find("pickaxe") then
                currentName = item:getName()
                pcall(function() currentIndex = item:directory()[item:getName()].index or 0 end)
                break
            end
        end
    end
    return "Equipped Axe: " .. currentName .. " | Index: " .. tostring(currentIndex)
end
function buildFarmStatusText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Farms: loading..." end
    local owned, ready = 0, 0
    if type(data.farms) == "table" then
        for farmId in pairs(data.farms) do
            owned = owned + 1
            if isFarmReadyToClaim(farmId, data) then ready = ready + 1 end
        end
    end
    return "Owned farms: " .. tostring(owned) .. " | Ready to claim: " .. tostring(ready) .. " | Gems: " .. formatShortNumber(getCurrency(data, "gems"))
end
function buildPetInventoryStatusText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Pets: loading..." end
    local total, equipped = 0, 0
    if data.inventory and data.inventory.pet then
        for _, raw in pairs(data.inventory.pet) do total = total + (tonumber(raw.am) or 1) end
    end
    if data.equippedPets then for _ in pairs(data.equippedPets) do equipped = equipped + 1 end end
    return "Pets owned: " .. tostring(total) .. " | Equipped: " .. tostring(equipped)
end
function buildAngelQuestStatusText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Angel Quest: loading..." end
    if not AngelQuests then return "Angel Quest: no data" end
    local tier = tonumber(data.angelQuestTier) or 1
    local total = #AngelQuests
    if tier > total then return "Angel Quest: completed all " .. tostring(total) end
    local info = AngelQuests[tier]
    if not info or not info.quest then return "Angel Quest: tier " .. tostring(tier) end
    local quest = info.quest
    local questType = getQuestType(quest) or "unknown"
    local progress = tonumber(data.angelQuestProgress) or 0
    local required = getQuestRequired(quest)
    return "Angel Quest: " .. tostring(questType) .. " | Tier " .. tostring(tier) .. "/" .. tostring(total) .. " | " .. tostring(progress) .. "/" .. tostring(required)
end

end

function buildHiveDetailedStatusText()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "Hive: loading..." end
    local honey = 0; local honeyItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, "honey")
    if honeyItem then honey = honeyItem:getAmount() end
    local toCollect = data.honeyToCollect or 0
    local equipped, totalBees = 0, 0
    if data.equippedBees then for _ in pairs(data.equippedBees) do equipped = equipped + 1 end end
    if data.inventory and data.inventory.bee then for _, bee in pairs(data.inventory.bee) do totalBees = totalBees + (bee.am or 1) end end
    local beedex = getAmountInIndexTable and getAmountInIndexTable(data.beedex) or 0
    return string.format("Honey: %s | To collect: %s | Bees: %d equipped / %d owned | Beedex: %d", formatShortNumber(honey), formatShortNumber(toCollect), equipped, totalBees, beedex)
end
function getMiniChestZoneOptions()
    local options = {}
    for groupName in pairs(miniChestList or {}) do addUnique(options, tostring(groupName)) end
    table.sort(options)
    if #options == 0 then table.insert(options, "All Zones") end
    table.insert(options, 1, "All Zones")
    return options
end
function claimSelectedMiniChestZonesStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedMiniChestZones"])
    local useAll = #selected == 0 or selected[1] == "All Zones"
    local data = getData()
    for _, chest in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("MiniChest")) do
        local groupName = chest:GetAttribute("miniChestId")
        if useAll or hasValue(selected, tostring(groupName)) then
            if canClaimMiniChest(chest, data) then
                local prompt = chest:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt", true)
                if prompt and fireproximityprompt then pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(prompt) end)
                else safeServiceCall(RewardService, "claimMiniChest", groupName, chest:GetAttribute("miniChestName")) end
                task.wait(0.05)
            end
        end
    end
end
function autoPickupGroundItemsStep()
    local hrp = getHRP()
    if not hrp then return end
    for _, inst in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
        if inst:IsA("ProximityPrompt") and inst.Enabled and inst.ObjectText ~= "Supply Drop" then
            local part = inst.Parent
            if part and part:IsA("BasePart") then
                local dist = (part.Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude
                if dist <= (tonumber(Library.Flags["PickupRange"]) or 25) then
                    if fireproximityprompt then pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(inst) end) end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function pickupStarsStep()
    for _, star in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("FallingStar")) do
        safeServiceCall(FallingStarsService, "claimStar", star.Name)
        task.wait(0.05)
    end
    for _, star in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Star")) do
        local prompt = star:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt", true)
        if prompt and fireproximityprompt then pcall(function() fireproximityprompt(prompt) end) end
        task.wait(0.05)
    end
end
function completeTutorialStep()
    safeServiceCall(RewardService, "completeTutorial")
    safeServiceCall(QuestService, "completeTutorial")
    pcall(function() local data = getData() if data then data.tutorialCompleted = true end end)
end
function loadMachineScriptOnce()
    pcall(function() loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/BigBeanLUA/RCU/refs/heads/main/Machine"))() end)
end
function getBuildingCraftNameOptions()
    local options = {}

    for buildingId, info in pairs(BuildingsList or {}) do
        if not data or not data.buildings or not data.buildings[buildingId] then
            table.insert(options, info.name or humanizeToken(buildingId))
        end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options
end
function autoCraftSelectedBuildingsStep()
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedBuildingsToCraft"])
    local idByName = {}
    for buildingId, info in pairs(BuildingsList or {}) do
        idByName[info.name or humanizeToken(buildingId)] = buildingId
    end
    local targets = selected
    if #targets == 0 then for buildingId in pairs(BuildingsList or {}) do table.insert(targets, buildingId) end end
    local data = getData()
    local neededOres = {}
    for _, label in ipairs(targets) do
        local buildingId = idByName[label]
        if buildingId and data then
            local buildingData = BuildingsList[buildingId]
            if buildingData and not (data.buildings and data.buildings[buildingId]) then
                local canAfford = true
                if buildingData.required then
                    for _, requiredItem in ipairs(buildingData.required) do
                        local itemName = type(requiredItem) == "table" and (requiredItem.nm or requiredItem.name or requiredItem:getName and requiredItem:getName() or "") or ""
                        local requiredAmount = type(requiredItem) == "table" and (requiredItem.am or requiredItem.amount or requiredItem:getAmount and requiredItem:getAmount() or 1) or 1
                        local currentItem = itemUtils and itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, itemName)
                        local currentAmount = currentItem and (type(currentItem.getAmount) == "function" and currentItem:getAmount() or currentItem.am or 1) or 0
                        if currentAmount < requiredAmount then
                            canAfford = false
                            if itemName:lower():find("ore") then
                                table.insert(neededOres, itemName)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if canAfford then
                    safeServiceCall(BuildingService, "build", buildingId)
                    task.wait(0.2)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if #neededOres > 0 then
        local sel = {}
        local oreList = _G.ORE_NAME_OPTIONS or {}
        for _, needed in ipairs(neededOres) do
            local neededLower = needed:lower():gsub(" ore$", "")
            for _, oreName in ipairs(oreList) do
                local oreClean = oreName:gsub("%[AFK%] ", ""):lower():gsub(" ore$", "")
                if oreClean == neededLower or oreClean:find(neededLower, 1, true) then
                    sel[oreName] = true
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        if next(sel) then
            Library.Flags["SelectedOres"] = sel
            if not Library.Flags["AutoMineOres"] and not Library.Flags["AutoMineOresTeleport"] then
                Library.Flags["AutoMineOres"] = true
            end
        end
    end
end
function getAngelQuestDiceOptions()
    local options = {}
    local auraDices = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Items", "AuraDices" }, "AuraDices") or {}
    for _, info in pairs(auraDices) do addUnique(options, info.name or "Dice") end
    table.sort(options)
    return options
end
function buildStatsEmbedFields()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return {} end
    local fields = {}
    local categories = Library.Flags["StatsWebhookCategories"]
    local selected = type(categories) == "table" and categories or {}
    local function include(key) return #readSelectedDropdownValues(selected) == 0 or hasValue(selected, key) end
    if include("Currencies") then
        table.insert(fields, { Name = "Currencies", Value = "Clicks: " .. formatShortNumber(getCurrency(data, "clicks")) .. "\nGems: " .. formatShortNumber(getCurrency(data, "gems")), Inline = true })
    end
    if include("Rebirths") then table.insert(fields, { Name = "Rebirths", Value = tostring(data.rebirths or 0), Inline = true }) end
    if include("Session") then table.insert(fields, { Name = "Session", Value = getSessionDurationText() .. "\nHatches: " .. tostring(RCUSessionStats.Hatches or 0), Inline = true }) end
    return fields
end
function sendRCUStatsWebhook(manual)
    local url = Library.Flags["RCUWebhookUrl"]
    if (not url or url == "") and not manual then return false end
    if not request then return false end
    local fields = buildStatsEmbedFields()
    if #fields == 0 then return false end
    local payload = {
        username = "Versus Airlines RCU",
        embeds = {{
            title = client.Name .. " • RCU Stats",
            color = 3447003,
            fields = fields,
            footer = { text = "VERSUS AIRLINES • Stats • Cammy / Aditya" },
            timestamp = DateTime.now():ToIsoDate(),
        }},
    }
    local ok = pcall(function()
        request({
            Url = url, Method = "POST",
            Headers = { ["Content-Type"] = "application/json" },
            Body = HttpService:JSONEncode(payload),
        })
    end)
    return ok
end
function startStatsWebhookInterval()
    Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag("RCU_StatsWebhook")
    if not Library.Flags["AutoSendStatsWebhook"] then return end
    local intervalMinutes = math.max(tonumber(Library.Flags["StatsWebhookInterval"]) or 30, 5)
    local last = 0
    local conn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if not Library.Flags["AutoSendStatsWebhook"] then return end
        if os.clock() - last < intervalMinutes * 60 then return end
        last = os.clock()
        sendRCUStatsWebhook(false)
    end)
    Library:TrackConnection(conn, "RCU_StatsWebhook")
end
function getIndexVariantOptions()
    local opts, map = {}, {}
    local TIER_NAMES = { "Normal", "Golden", "Toxic", "Galaxy" }
    for ti, tn in ipairs(TIER_NAMES) do
        table.insert(opts, tn)
        map[tn] = { Tier = ti, Shiny = false, RarityGroup = "STANDARD" }
    end
    for _, rg in ipairs({ "Eternal", "Secret" }) do
        for ti, tn in ipairs(TIER_NAMES) do
            local dn = tn .. " " .. rg
            table.insert(opts, dn)
            map[dn] = { Tier = ti, Shiny = false, RarityGroup = rg }
        end
    end
    return opts, map
end
autoIndexRunning = false
autoIndexThread = nil
autoIndexOriginalSettings = {}
function startAutoIndexThread()
        if autoIndexThread then task.cancel(autoIndexThread); autoIndexThread = nil end
        autoIndexThread = task.spawn(function()
            local EggsModule = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Eggs" }, "Pets.Eggs") or {}
            local Pets = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Pets" }, "Pets.Pets") or {}
            local variantOpts, variantMap = getIndexVariantOptions()

            local VARIANT_OPTIONS = {}
            for _, dn in ipairs(variantOpts) do
                local v = variantMap[dn]
                if v then table.insert(VARIANT_OPTIONS, { Name = dn, Tier = v.Tier, Shiny = v.Shiny, RarityGroup = v.RarityGroup }) end
            end

            while autoIndexRunning do
                local selectedVariantsArr = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedIndexVariants"])
                local selectedEggsArr = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedIndexEggs"])
                local selectedVariants, selectedEggs = {}, {}
                for _, v in ipairs(selectedVariantsArr) do selectedVariants[v] = true end
                for _, v in ipairs(selectedEggsArr) do selectedEggs[v] = true end
                if not next(selectedVariants) then
                    for _, dn in ipairs(variantOpts) do selectedVariants[dn] = true end
                end

                -- Gather eggs to process
                local allEggs = {}
                if not next(selectedEggs) then
                    for name, data in pairs(EggsModule) do
                        if data.pets and not name:find("Exclusive") then table.insert(allEggs, { Name = name, Data = data }) end
                    end
                else
                    for eggName, isSelected in pairs(selectedEggs) do
                        if isSelected and EggsModule[eggName] then table.insert(allEggs, { Name = eggName, Data = EggsModule[eggName] }) end
                    end
                end
                table.sort(allEggs, function(a, b) return (a.Data.requiredMap or 0) < (b.Data.requiredMap or 0) end)

                for _, eggInfo in ipairs(allEggs) do
                    if not autoIndexRunning then break end
                    local currentEggName, currentEggData = eggInfo.Name, eggInfo.Data

                    while autoIndexRunning do
                        local playerData = getData()
                        if not playerData then task.wait(1); continue end

                        local highestMap = 0
                        if playerData.maps then
                            for mapId, _ in pairs(playerData.maps) do
                                local numId = tonumber(mapId)
                                if numId and numId > highestMap then highestMap = numId end
                            end
                        end
                        local requiredMap = currentEggData.requiredMap or 0
                        local isUnlocked = highestMap >= requiredMap
                        if not isUnlocked then break end

                        local playerIndex = playerData.index or {}
                        local goals = {}
                        local needsToCraft = {}

                        for petName, _ in pairs(currentEggData.pets) do
                            if type(petName) ~= "string" or not Pets[petName] then continue end
                            local petDef = Pets[petName]
                            if petDef.rarity == "Divine" or petDef.rarity == "Supreme" or petDef.rarity == "Ultimate" then continue end

                            for _, variant in ipairs(VARIANT_OPTIONS) do
                                if selectedVariants[variant.Name] then
                                    if variant.Name:find("Galaxy") then
                                        local MapsModule = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Maps" }, "Maps") or {}
                                        local reqMap = currentEggData.requiredMap or 0
                                        local worldNum = 1
                                        if reqMap and MapsModule[reqMap] and MapsModule[reqMap].world then
                                            worldNum = MapsModule[reqMap].world
                                        end
                                        if worldNum < 2 then continue end
                                    end

                                    local rarityMatch = (variant.RarityGroup == "STANDARD" and petDef.rarity ~= "Eternal" and petDef.rarity ~= "Secret") or (variant.RarityGroup == petDef.rarity)
                                    if rarityMatch then
                                        local isMissing = true
                                        local descriptor = petName:lower():gsub(" ", "") .. ":" .. variant.Tier .. (variant.Shiny and ":s" or "")
                                        if playerIndex[descriptor] then isMissing = false end
                                        if isMissing then
                                            table.insert(goals, variant.Name .. " " .. petName)
                                            if variant.Tier and variant.Tier > 1 then
                                                needsToCraft[petName .. ":" .. (variant.Tier - 1) .. (variant.Shiny and ":s" or "")] = true
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        if #goals == 0 then
                            if indexStatusLabel then setVersusLabelText(indexStatusLabel, "Egg '" .. currentEggName .. "' complete! Moving to next...") end
                            task.wait(2); break
                        end

                        if indexStatusLabel then setVersusLabelText(indexStatusLabel, "Working on Egg: " .. currentEggName .. "\nIndexing: " .. table.concat(goals, ", ")) end

                        -- Craft owned pets (5+ copies) that are needed
                        local shouldCraftNow = false
                        local ownedForCrafting = {}
                        for petName, _ in pairs(currentEggData.pets) do
                            local petIdsForName = {}
                            for pid, raw in pairs(playerData.inventory.pet or {}) do
                                local petObject = itemUtils.createItemFromData and itemUtils.createItemFromData(raw)
                                if petObject then
                                    local pn = petObject:getName()
                                    if pn == petName then
                                        petIdsForName[pid] = raw
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            for pid, raw in pairs(petIdsForName) do
                                local amt = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.am or 0) or 0
                                if amt >= 5 then
                                    ownedForCrafting[pid] = true
                                    shouldCraftNow = true
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        if shouldCraftNow then
                            for pid, _ in pairs(ownedForCrafting) do
                                if not autoIndexRunning then break end
                                local ok = pcall(function() PetService:craft({ [1] = pid }, false, 1) end)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end

                        local currency = currentEggData.currency or "clicks"
                        local balance = getCurrency(playerData, currency) or 0
                        local isAffordable = balance >= (currentEggData.cost or 0)

                        if isAffordable then
                            local currentSelected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedEgg"])
                            if currentSelected ~= currentEggName or not Library.Flags["AutoHatchSelectedEgg"] then
                                Library.Flags["SelectedEgg"] = currentEggName
                                eggDropdown:updateList(getEggNames(false))
                                Library.Flags["SelectedHatchAmount"] = "Max"
                                Library.Flags["AutoHatchSelectedEgg"] = true
                                Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag("RCU_AutoHatchSelectedEgg")
                                interval("RCU_AutoHatchSelectedEgg", "AutoHatchSelectedEgg", 0.35, function()
                                    local se = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedEgg"], "None")
                                    local en, em = resolveEggSelection(se)
                                    if en and en ~= "None" then openEgg(en, em) end
                                end)
                            end
                        else
                            if Library.Flags["AutoHatchSelectedEgg"] then
                                Library.Flags["AutoHatchSelectedEgg"] = false
                                Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag("RCU_AutoHatchSelectedEgg")
                            end
                            if indexStatusLabel then setVersusLabelText(indexStatusLabel, "Not enough " .. currency .. " for '" .. currentEggName .. "'. Skipping...") end
                            task.wait(2); break
                        end

                        task.wait(5)
                    end
                end

                if not autoIndexRunning then break end
                if indexStatusLabel then setVersusLabelText(indexStatusLabel, "Cycle complete. Re-checking in 5 seconds...") end
                task.wait(5)
            end
        end)
    end

function getRingOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    for ringId, ringData in pairs(RingsList or {}) do
        if type(ringData) ~= "table" or ringData.expired ~= true then
            local name = type(ringData) == "table" and (ringData.name or humanizeToken(ringId)) or humanizeToken(ringId)
            table.insert(options, name)
            map[name] = ringId
        end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end

        end
    end

    return options, map

function getMagicPotOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local potList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "MagicPot" }, "MagicPot") or {}
    for id, recipe in pairs(potList) do
        local item = recipe.item
        if item then
            local name = item.nm or "Unknown"
            local cls = item.cl or ""
            local display = name .. (cls ~= "" and " (" .. cls .. ")" or "")
            table.insert(options, display)
            map[display] = { id = id, name = name, recipe = recipe }
        end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end
function getJungleForgeWoodOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.mapItem then return options, map end
    local trees = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Trees" }, "Trees") or {}
    for itemId, itemData in pairs(data.inventory.mapItem) do
        local item = itemUtils.createItemFromData and itemUtils.createItemFromData(itemData)
        if item and item.usableInJungleForge and item:usableInJungleForge() then
            local name = item:getName() or "Unknown"
            local amount = item:getAmount() or 0
            if amount >= 200 and name ~= "" then
                table.insert(options, name)
                map[name] = itemId
            end
        end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end
function canJungleForgeToday()
    local data = getData()
    return data and (tonumber(data.jungleForgeCrafts) or 0) < 50
end
function getLumberjackMapOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local maps = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Maps" }, "Maps") or {}
    for mapId, mapData in pairs(maps) do
        if mapData.lumberjack then
            table.insert(options, mapData.name or humanizeToken(mapId))
            map[mapData.name or humanizeToken(mapId)] = mapId
        end
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end
function getLumberjackItemOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local items = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Lumberjack", "Items" }, "Lumberjack.Items") or {}
    for itemId, itemData in pairs(items) do
        local baseName = itemData.item and itemData.item:getName() or "Unknown"
        for amt = 1, itemData.max or 1 do
            local display = baseName .. " " .. tostring(amt) .. "x"
            table.insert(options, display)
            map[display] = { itemId = itemId, amount = amt }
        end
    end
    table.sort(options, function(a, b)
        local aItem, aAmt = a:match("^(.+) (%d+)x$")
        local bItem, bAmt = b:match("^(.+) (%d+)x$")
        if aItem == bItem then return tonumber(aAmt) < tonumber(bAmt) end
        return (aItem or "") < (bItem or "")
    end)
    return options, map
end
function getAdjustedLumberjackItems()
    local adjusted = {}
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedLumberjackItems"])
    local _, itemMap = getLumberjackItemOptions()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return adjusted end
    local highest = {}
    for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
        local info = itemMap[display]
        if info then
            local baseName = display:match("^(.+) %d+x$") or display
            if not highest[baseName] or info.amount > highest[baseName].amount then
                highest[baseName] = info
            end
        end
    end
    for _, info in pairs(highest) do
        local itemName = nil
        local itemsDef = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Lumberjack", "Items" }, "Lumberjack.Items") or {}
        local itemDef = itemsDef[info.itemId]
        if itemDef and itemDef.item then itemName = itemDef.item:getName() end
        local playerAmt = 0
        if itemName then
            local item = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, itemName)
            if item then playerAmt = item:getAmount() or 0 end
        end
        adjusted[tostring(info.itemId)] = math.min(info.amount, playerAmt)
    end
    return adjusted
end
function isLumberjackWorking()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return "idle" end
    local rewards = data.lumberjackRewards or {}
    local finished = data.lumberjackFinished or 0
    if #rewards > 0 and os.time() >= finished then return "ready_to_claim" end
    if os.time() < finished then return "working" end
    return "idle"
end
function canAffordLumberjackUpgrade()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return false end
    local upgrades = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Lumberjack", "Upgrades" }, "Lumberjack.Upgrades") or {}
    local current = data.lumberjackUpgrades or 0
    local nextUp = upgrades[current + 1]
    return nextUp and getCurrency(data, "gems") >= (nextUp.price or 0)
end

    end

function getSteampunkItemOptions(upgradeId)
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local sp = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "SteampunkMachine" }, "SteampunkMachine") or {}
    local data = sp[upgradeId]
    if data and data.items then
        for i, item in ipairs(data.items) do
            local name = item.nm or "Unknown"
            local amt = item.am or 1
            local display = name .. " (" .. tostring(amt) .. "x)"
            table.insert(options, display)
            map[display] = { index = i, name = name, amount = amt }
        end
    end
    return options, map
end
function hasSteampunkBoost(upgradeId)
    local data = getData()
    if not data or not data.activeBoosts then return false end
    for boostName, timeLeft in pairs(data.activeBoosts) do
        if boostName == upgradeId .. "Steampunk" and timeLeft > 0 then return true end
    end
    return false
end
function getLunarForgeOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local lunar = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "LunarForge" }, "LunarForge") or {}
    local sorted = {}
    for id, data in pairs(lunar) do
        local name = data.item and data.item:getName() or "Unknown"
        table.insert(sorted, { id = tonumber(id) or id, name = name, data = data })
    end
    table.sort(sorted, function(a, b) return tonumber(a.id) < tonumber(b.id) end)
    for _, entry in ipairs(sorted) do
        table.insert(options, entry.name)
        map[entry.name] = { id = entry.id, item = entry.data.item, requiredAmount = entry.data.item and (entry.data.item:getAmount() or 1) or 1 }
    end
    return options, map
end
function getSpaceCrateOptions()

    for id, data in pairs(crates) do
        table.insert(sorted, { id = tonumber(id) or id, name = (data.name or "Unknown") .. " Crate", price = data.price or 0 })

    for _, entry in ipairs(sorted) do

    end

end
function getRelicOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local relics = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Space", "RelicsUpgrader" }, "Space.RelicsUpgrader") or {}
    for id, data in pairs(relics) do
        local name = data.item and data.item:getName() or humanizeToken(id)
        table.insert(options, name)
        map[name] = { id = id, data = data }
    end
    table.sort(options)
    return options, map
end
function getSpaceUpgradeOptions()

    local upgrades = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Space", "Upgrades" }, "Space.Upgrades") or {}
    for id, data in pairs(upgrades) do
        local name = data.name or humanizeToken(id)

    end

    return options, map
end

function getPickaxeRuneOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local runes = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "PickaxeRunes" }, "Mine.PickaxeRunes")
    if type(runes) == "table" then
        for id, data in pairs(runes) do
            local name = data.name or humanizeToken(id)
            table.insert(options, name)
            map[name] = id
        end
        table.sort(options)
    end
    if #options == 0 then
        local data = getData()
        if data and data.inventory then
            for _, key in ipairs({ "rune", "runes" }) do
                local container = data.inventory[key]
                if type(container) == "table" then
                    for runeId in pairs(container) do
                        local name = humanizeToken(runeId)
                        table.insert(options, name)
                        map[name] = runeId
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        table.sort(options)
    end
    return options, map
end


-- Underground Market helpers

function getUndergroundMarketOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local umList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "UndergroundMarket" }, "Mine.UndergroundMarket") or {}
    for i, entry in ipairs(umList) do
        local itemAmt = entry.item and (entry.item.am or (typeof(entry.item.getAmount) == "function" and entry.item:getAmount()) or entry.item.amount or 1)
        local itemName = entry.item and (entry.item.nm or (typeof(entry.item.getName) == "function" and entry.item:getName()) or "Unknown")
        local priceAmt = entry.price and (entry.price.am or (typeof(entry.price.getAmount) == "function" and entry.price:getAmount()) or entry.price.amount or 1)
        local priceName = entry.price and (entry.price.nm or (typeof(entry.price.getName) == "function" and entry.price:getName()) or "Unknown")
        local display = tostring(itemAmt) .. "x " .. tostring(itemName) .. " - " .. tostring(priceAmt) .. "x " .. tostring(priceName)
        table.insert(options, display)
        map[display] = { index = i, item = entry.item, price = entry.price }
    end
    return options, map
end

function autoBuyUndergroundMarketStep(count)
    count = count or 5
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local umList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "UndergroundMarket" }, "Mine.UndergroundMarket") or {}
    local Functions = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "Functions" }, "Functions")
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedMarketItems"])
    local _, map = getUndergroundMarketOptions()
    if #selected == 0 then return end
    local player = Players.LocalPlayer
    local seed = function(p22)
        local serverTime = (Knit and Knit.serverTimeNow) or os.time()
        local t = DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(serverTime + 3600):ToUniversalTime()
        local s = t.Year * 222 + t.Month * 333 + t.Day * 444444 + t.Hour * 33333
        local ms = math.floor(t.Minute / 10)
        return s + ms * 555 + player.UserId + p22
    end
    for i = 1, count do
        local s = seed(i)
        local itemData = Functions and umList[Functions.getRandom and Functions.getRandom(umList, s)] or umList[1]
        if not itemData then continue end
        local itemAmt = itemData.item and (itemData.item.am or (typeof(itemData.item.getAmount) == "function" and itemData.item:getAmount()) or itemData.item.amount or 1)
        local itemName = itemData.item and (itemData.item.nm or (typeof(itemData.item.getName) == "function" and itemData.item:getName()) or "Unknown")
        local priceAmt = itemData.price and (itemData.price.am or (typeof(itemData.price.getAmount) == "function" and itemData.price:getAmount()) or itemData.price.amount or 1)
        local priceName = itemData.price and (itemData.price.nm or (typeof(itemData.price.getName) == "function" and itemData.price:getName()) or "Unknown")
        local display = tostring(itemAmt) .. "x " .. tostring(itemName) .. " - " .. tostring(priceAmt) .. "x " .. tostring(priceName)
        local isSelected = false
        for _, sel in ipairs(selected) do
            if sel == display then isSelected = true break end
        end
        if not isSelected then continue end
        local priceItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, priceName)
        local owned = priceItem and priceItem:getAmount() or 0
        local affordable = owned >= priceAmt
        local bought = data.undergroundMarketBought or {}
        local inStock = not bought[tostring(s)]
        if inStock and affordable then
            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "buyUndergroundMarket", i)
        end
    end
end


-- Ore Processor helpers

function getProcessorTierOptions()
    local options, map = {}, {}
    local processor = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "OresProcessor" }, "Mine.OresProcessor") or {}
    for id in pairs(processor) do
        if type(id) == "number" then
            table.insert(options, tostring(id))
            map[tostring(id)] = id
        end
    end
    table.sort(options, function(a, b) return tonumber(a) < tonumber(b) end)
    return options, map
end

function autoProcessOresStep(count)
    count = count or 10
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local processor = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "OresProcessor" }, "Mine.OresProcessor") or {}
    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedProcessorTiers"])
    if #selected == 0 then return end
    for _, tierStr in ipairs(selected) do
        local tier = tonumber(tierStr)
        if not tier then continue end
        local pData = processor[tier]
        if not pData or not pData.required then continue end
        local maxCraftable = math.huge
        for _, req in ipairs(pData.required) do
            local rName = req:getName()
            local rAmt = req:getAmount()
            local item = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, rName)
            local have = item and item:getAmount() or 0
            maxCraftable = math.min(maxCraftable, math.floor(have / rAmt))
        end
        if maxCraftable > 0 and maxCraftable ~= math.huge then
            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "oreProcessor", tier, maxCraftable)
        end
    end
end


-- Season Quest auto-complete helpers

_G.CurrentResourceQuest = _G.CurrentResourceQuest or nil
_G.SmartHatchDelay = _G.SmartHatchDelay or nil

SeasonQuestState = SeasonQuestState or {
    selectedQuestEgg = nil,
    selectedMythicalEternalEgg = nil,
    selectedAuraDice = {},
    selectedQuests = {},
    eggOptions = {},
    displayToEggName = {},
    questOptions = {},
    busying = false,
    busyUntil = 0,
}

function getValidSeasonFolder()
    local season = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
    local seasonObj = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.List:FindFirstChild("Season" .. tostring(season))
    if not seasonObj then return nil end
    if seasonObj:IsA("Folder") then
        local preferred = seasonObj:FindFirstChild("Quests")
        if preferred and preferred:IsA("ModuleScript") then return preferred end
        local fallback = seasonObj:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ModuleScript")
        if fallback then return fallback end
    end
    if seasonObj:IsA("ModuleScript") then return seasonObj end
    return nil
end

function getQuestModule()
    local obj = getValidSeasonFolder()
    if not obj then return nil end
    local ok, mod = pcall(require, obj)
    if not ok or type(mod) ~= "table" then return nil end
    return mod.Quests or mod
end

function formatPercent(value)
    value = tonumber(value) or 0
    local formatted = string.format("%.6f", value)
    formatted = formatted:gsub("0+$", "")
    formatted = formatted:gsub("%.$", "")
    return formatted .. "%"
end

function getActiveTreesInGroup(groupId, data)
    local treesWithHealth = {}
    local mapsFolder = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Game") and Workspace.Game:FindFirstChild("Maps")
    if not mapsFolder or not data or not data.trees then return treesWithHealth end
    local mapName
    for _, map in pairs(mapsFolder:GetChildren()) do
        if map.Name:lower() == groupId:lower() then mapName = map.Name break end
    end
    if not mapName then return treesWithHealth end
    local treesFolder = mapsFolder[mapName]:FindFirstChild("Trees")
    if not treesFolder then return treesWithHealth end
    for _, tree in pairs(treesFolder:GetChildren()) do
        local treeId = tree:GetAttribute("treeId")
        local hasModel = tree:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Model") ~= nil
        if treeId and hasModel and data.trees[groupId] and data.trees[groupId][treeId]
            and data.trees[groupId][treeId].hp > 0 and not data.trees[groupId][treeId].respawn then
            table.insert(treesWithHealth, {
                treeId = treeId, hp = data.trees[groupId][treeId].hp,
                instance = tree, groupId = groupId
            })
        end
    end
    table.sort(treesWithHealth, function(a, b) return a.hp < b.hp end)
    return treesWithHealth
end

function getBestEggs()
    local EggData = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Eggs" }, "Pets.Eggs") or {}
    local PetData = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Pets" }, "Pets.Pets") or {}
    local scores = {}
    for eggName, eggInfo in pairs(EggData) do
        local pets = eggInfo.pets
        if type(pets) ~= "table" then break end
        local score = { Eternal = 0, Mythical = 0 }
        for petName, chance in pairs(pets) do
            local petInfo = PetData[petName]
            if petInfo and petInfo.rarity then
                if petInfo.rarity == "Eternal" then score.Eternal = score.Eternal + chance
                elseif petInfo.rarity == "Mythical" then score.Mythical = score.Mythical + chance end
            end
        end
        local combined = score.Eternal + score.Mythical
        if combined > 0 then
            table.insert(scores, {
                name = eggName, eternal = score.Eternal, mythical = score.Mythical,
                combined = combined, cost = eggInfo.cost or 0, currency = eggInfo.currency or "clicks"
            })
        end
    end
    table.sort(scores, function(a, b) return a.cost < b.cost end)
    return scores
end

function getSeasonEggList()
    local EggData = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Eggs" }, "Pets.Eggs") or {}
    local eggsTable, displayToEggName = {}, {}
    for eggName, eggData in pairs(EggData) do
        if typeof(eggData) == "table" and eggData.cost then
            table.insert(eggsTable, {name = eggName, cost = eggData.cost, currency = eggData.currency or "clicks"})
        end
    end
    table.sort(eggsTable, function(a, b) return a.cost < b.cost end)
    local eggOptions = {}
    for _, eggInfo in ipairs(eggsTable) do
        local displayName = eggInfo.name .. " - " .. formatShortNumber(eggInfo.cost) .. " " .. eggInfo.currency
        table.insert(eggOptions, displayName)
        displayToEggName[displayName] = eggInfo.name
    end
    table.insert(eggOptions, "Best Egg (Clicks)")
    SeasonQuestState.eggOptions = eggOptions
    SeasonQuestState.displayToEggName = displayToEggName
    return eggOptions, displayToEggName
end

function getAllSeasonQuests()
    local questOptions = {}
    local mod = getQuestModule()
    if mod then
        for difficulty, questList in pairs(mod) do
            if type(questList) == "table" then
                for questId, questInfo in pairs(questList) do
                    if questInfo and questInfo.quest then
                        local questType = questInfo.quest.quest
                        if questType then
                            table.insert(questOptions, string.format("[%s] %s", tostring(difficulty):upper(), questType))
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    table.sort(questOptions)
    SeasonQuestState.questOptions = questOptions
    return questOptions
end

function getAuraDiceList()
    local diceList = {}
    local AuraDices = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Items", "AuraDices" }, "Items.AuraDices") or {}
    for diceId, diceData in pairs(AuraDices) do
        if diceData.name then table.insert(diceList, diceData.name) end
    end
    table.sort(diceList)
    return diceList
end

function getPickaxeDamage()
    local data = getData()
    if data and data.inventory and data.inventory.exclusive then
        local ExclusiveItems = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Items", "Exclusive" }, "Items.Exclusive") or {}
        for _, itemData in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
            local itemName = type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name) or ""
            if itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") then
                local pickaxeData = ExclusiveItems[itemName]
                if pickaxeData and pickaxeData.multiplier then
                    return pickaxeData.multiplier + (data.pickaxeDamageMultiplier or 0)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return 10
end

function findBestRoomForOre(oreId, pickaxeDamage)
    local Ores = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "Ores" }, "Mine.Ores") or {}
    local OreRooms = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "OreRooms" }, "Mine.OreRooms") or {}
    local bestRoom, bestChance = nil, 0
    for roomName, roomData in pairs(OreRooms) do
        if roomData.ores and roomData.ores[oreId] then
            local oreChance = roomData.ores[oreId]
            local totalChance, unbeatableChance = 0, 0
            for roomOreId, chance in pairs(roomData.ores) do
                totalChance = totalChance + chance
                local roomOreData = Ores[roomOreId]
                if roomOreData and roomOreData.hp then
                    if math.ceil(roomOreData.hp / pickaxeDamage) > 75 then
                        unbeatableChance = unbeatableChance + chance
                    end
                end
            end
            local unbeatablePercent = totalChance > 0 and (unbeatableChance / totalChance) * 100 or 0
            if unbeatablePercent <= 20 and oreChance > bestChance then
                bestChance = oreChance
                bestRoom = roomName
            end
        end
    end
    return bestRoom
end

function findBestRoomForOres(selectedOreIds, pickaxeDamage)
    local Ores = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "Ores" }, "Mine.Ores") or {}
    local OreRooms = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "OreRooms" }, "Mine.OreRooms") or {}
    local bestRoom, bestScore = nil, 0
    local fallbackRoom, fallbackScore = nil, 0
    for roomName, roomData in pairs(OreRooms) do
        if roomData.ores then
            local totalSelectedChance = 0
            for _, oreId in ipairs(selectedOreIds) do
                if roomData.ores[oreId] then
                    totalSelectedChance = totalSelectedChance + roomData.ores[oreId]
                end
            end
            if totalSelectedChance > 0 then
                local totalChance, beatableChance = 0, 0
                for roomOreId, chance in pairs(roomData.ores) do
                    totalChance = totalChance + chance
                    local roomOreData = Ores[roomOreId]
                    if roomOreData and roomOreData.hp then
                        if math.ceil(roomOreData.hp / pickaxeDamage) <= 75 then
                            beatableChance = beatableChance + chance
                        end
                    end
                end
                local beatablePercent = totalChance > 0 and (beatableChance / totalChance) * 100 or 0
                if totalSelectedChance > fallbackScore then
                    fallbackScore = totalSelectedChance
                    fallbackRoom = roomName
                end
                if beatablePercent > 25 and totalSelectedChance > bestScore then
                    bestScore = totalSelectedChance
                    bestRoom = roomName
                end
            end
        end
    end
    return bestRoom or fallbackRoom
end

RoomOptimizationState = RoomOptimizationState or { LastCheck = 0 }
function optimizeMineRoom()
    if os.clock() - RoomOptimizationState.LastCheck < 12 then return end
    RoomOptimizationState.LastCheck = os.clock()
    local selectedOres = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedOres"])
    if #selectedOres == 0 then return end
    local Ores = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "Ores" }, "Mine.Ores") or {}
    local rawNames = {}
    for _, sel in ipairs(selectedOres) do
        local clean = sel:gsub("%[AFK%] ", "")
        for rawName in pairs(Ores) do
            local formatted = humanizeToken(rawName):gsub(" Ore$", "")
            if formatted == clean or rawName:lower():find(clean:lower(), 1, true) then
                table.insert(rawNames, rawName)
                break
            end
        end
    end
    if #rawNames == 0 then return end
    local pickaxeDamage = getPickaxeDamage()
    local bestRoom = findBestRoomForOres(rawNames, pickaxeDamage)
    if bestRoom then
        local roomNumber = bestRoom:match("%d+")
        if roomNumber then
            Library.Flags["MineRoom"] = { roomNumber }
        end
    end
end

function resolveBestEgg(selectedEgg, eggOptions, displayToEggName)
    if selectedEgg == "Best Egg (Clicks)" then
        local EggData = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Eggs" }, "Pets.Eggs") or {}
        local data = getData()
        local highestMap = 0
        if data and data.maps then
            for mapNumber, _ in pairs(data.maps) do
                if tonumber(mapNumber) and tonumber(mapNumber) > highestMap then highestMap = tonumber(mapNumber) end
            end
        end
        for eggName, eggData in pairs(EggData) do
            if eggData.requiredMap == highestMap and (eggData.currency == "clicks" or not eggData.currency) then
                return eggName
            end
        end
    end
    return displayToEggName[selectedEgg] or (type(selectedEgg) == "string" and selectedEgg:match("^(.-) %-") or selectedEgg)
end


-- Sections / UI


-- Game teleport helpers

function getTeleportFrameComponent()
    if TeleportFrameComponent ~= nil then return TeleportFrameComponent end
    local playerScripts = client:FindFirstChild("PlayerScripts")
