    local module = findPath(playerScripts, { "Client", "Components", "UI", "Frames", "TeleportFrame" })
    TeleportFrameComponent = safeRequire(module, "Client.Components.UI.Frames.TeleportFrame")
    return TeleportFrameComponent
end

function getSpawnMapId()
    for mapId, mapData in pairs(MapList or {}) do
        if type(mapData) == "table" and tostring(mapData.name or ""):lower() == "spawn" then
            return mapId
        end
    end
    return 1
end

function getCurrentMapId()
    if MapController and MapController.getCurrentMap then
        local ok, mapId = pcall(function() return MapController:getCurrentMap(true) end)
        if ok and mapId ~= nil then return mapId end
    end
    local data = getData()
    if data and data.currentMap then return data.currentMap end
    return nil
end

function teleportToMapUsingGameController(mapId)
    mapId = tonumber(mapId) or mapId
    local mapData = MapList and MapList[mapId]
    if type(mapData) ~= "table" or typeof(mapData.cframe) ~= "CFrame" then return false end

    local teleportFrame = getTeleportFrameComponent()
    if teleportFrame and type(teleportFrame.teleportToPosition) == "function" then
        local ok = pcall(function()
            return teleportFrame:teleportToPosition(mapId, mapData.cframe)
        end)
        if ok then return true end
    end

    return false
end

function teleportToSpawnForQuest()
    local spawnMapId = getSpawnMapId()
    if tostring(getCurrentMapId() or "") == tostring(spawnMapId) then return true end

    if os.clock() - (QuestRuntimeState and QuestRuntimeState.lastSpawnTeleport or 0) < 18 then
        return false
    end

    QuestRuntimeState.lastSpawnTeleport = os.clock()
    return teleportToMapUsingGameController(spawnMapId)
end


-- Quest automation helpers

QuestListCache = QuestListCache or nil
QuestRuntimeState = QuestRuntimeState or {
    lastWallTouch = 0,
    lastQuestScan = 0,
    lastSpawnTeleport = 0,
}

function serviceCallSucceeded(result, err)
    if err ~= nil then return false end
    if result == nil then return true end
    if result == true or result == "success" then return true end
    if result == false then return false end
    if type(result) == "string" and result:lower():find("fail", 1, true) then return false end
    return true
end

function callFirstQuestMethod(service, methodNames, ...)
    for _, methodName in ipairs(methodNames or {}) do
        local result, err = safeServiceCall(service, methodName, ...)
        if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then
            return result, nil, methodName
        end
    end
    return nil, "missing_quest_method"
end

function getQuestType(quest)
    if type(quest) ~= "table" then return "" end
    return tostring(quest.quest or quest.type or quest.Type or quest.id or "")
end

function getQuestName(quest)
    if type(quest) ~= "table" then return nil end
    return quest.name or quest.Name or quest.target or quest.Target or quest.egg or quest.Egg or quest.item or quest.Item
end

function getQuestRequired(quest)
    if type(quest) ~= "table" then return 1 end
    local amount = quest.amount or quest.Amount or quest.required or quest.Required or quest.total or quest.Total
    if type(amount) == "table" then
        amount = amount[2] or amount[1]
    end
    return tonumber(amount) or 1
end

function getQuestProgress(container, questId, questData)
    if type(questData) == "table" then
        local direct = questData.progress or questData.Progress or questData.current or questData.Current or questData.amountDone or questData.AmountDone
        if tonumber(direct) then return tonumber(direct) end
    end
    if type(container) == "table" then
        local raw = container[questId] or container[tostring(questId)]
        if type(raw) == "number" then return raw end
        if type(raw) == "table" then
            return tonumber(raw.progress or raw.Progress or raw.current or raw.Current or raw.amountDone or raw.AmountDone) or 0
        end
    end
    return 0
end

function getCurrentMapQuest()
    local data = getData()
    if not data or type(data.maps) ~= "table" or type(MapList) ~= "table" then return nil end

    local nextMapId = #data.maps + 1
    local mapData = MapList[nextMapId]
    if not mapData or type(mapData.quests) ~= "table" then return nil, nil, mapData, nextMapId, false end
    if mapData.unlocksAt and os.time() < mapData.unlocksAt then return nil, nil, mapData, nextMapId, false end

    local allComplete = true
    for questId, quest in pairs(mapData.quests) do
        local progress = getQuestProgress(data.mapQuests, questId)
        if progress < getQuestRequired(quest) then
            allComplete = false
            return quest, questId, mapData, nextMapId, false, progress
        end
    end

    return nil, nil, mapData, nextMapId, allComplete
end

function findMapWallForMap(mapId)
    for _, wall in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("MapWall")) do
        if wall:GetAttribute("mapId") == mapId then
            return wall
        end
    end

    -- Fallback for executors/games where CollectionService tags are late to replicate.
    local checked = 0
    for _, inst in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
        checked = checked + 1
        if checked > 3500 then break end
        if inst:GetAttribute("mapId") == mapId and inst:FindFirstChild("UnlockGui") then
            return inst
        end
    end
    return nil
end

function touchMapWall(mapId)
    if os.clock() - (QuestRuntimeState.lastWallTouch or 0) < 3 then return false end
    QuestRuntimeState.lastWallTouch = os.clock()

    local wall = findMapWallForMap(mapId)
    if not wall then return false end
    local hrp = getHRP()
    local wallPart = getPart(wall)
    if not hrp or not wallPart then return false end

    local previousMapId = tonumber(mapId) and math.max(1, tonumber(mapId) - 1) or getSpawnMapId()
    if (hrp.Position - wallPart.Position).Magnitude > 90 then
        teleportToMapUsingGameController(previousMapId)
    end

    moveToPosition(wallPart.Position)

    local touchPart = wall:FindFirstChild("Touch", true) or wallPart
    if touchPart and firetouchinterest and (hrp.Position - wallPart.Position).Magnitude <= 14 then
        pcall(function()
            firetouchinterest(hrp, touchPart, 0)
            task.wait(0.05)
            firetouchinterest(hrp, touchPart, 1)
        end)
    end

    return true
end

function getPetRarityName(petName)
    local petData = type(PetsModule) == "table" and PetsModule[petName]
    if type(petData) == "table" and petData.rarity then
        return tostring(petData.rarity)
    end
    if petUtils and petUtils.getRarity then
        local ok, rarity = pcall(function() return petUtils.getRarity(petName) end)
        if ok and rarity then return tostring(rarity) end
    end
    return nil
end

function getEggForPetName(petName)
    if not petName or petName == "" then return nil end
    local bestEgg, bestCost = nil, -math.huge
    for eggName, eggData in pairs(EggsModule or {}) do
        if type(eggData) == "table" and type(eggData.pets) == "table" and eggData.pets[petName] then
            local cost = tonumber(eggData.cost) or 0
            if canAffordEgg(eggName) and cost > bestCost then
                bestEgg, bestCost = eggName, cost
            end
        end
    end
    return bestEgg
end

function getEggForPetRarity(rarityName)
    if not rarityName or rarityName == "" then return nil end
    local wanted = tostring(rarityName):lower()
    local bestEgg, bestCost = nil, -math.huge

    for eggName, eggData in pairs(EggsModule or {}) do
        if type(eggData) == "table" and type(eggData.pets) == "table" and canAffordEgg(eggName) then
            for petName in pairs(eggData.pets) do
                local rarity = getPetRarityName(petName)
                if rarity and rarity:lower() == wanted then
                    local cost = tonumber(eggData.cost) or 0
                    if cost > bestCost then
                        bestEgg, bestCost = eggName, cost
                    end
                    break
                end
            end
        end
    end

    return bestEgg
end

function questTypeToRarity(questType)
    local lower = tostring(questType or ""):lower()
    local rarities = {
        "common", "uncommon", "rare", "epic", "legendary", "mythical", "eternal", "mysterious", "exclusive", "secret", "divine", "supreme", "ultimate",
    }
    for _, rarity in ipairs(rarities) do
        if lower:find(rarity, 1, true) then
            return rarity:gsub("^%l", string.upper)
        end
    end
    return nil
end

function openQuestEgg(quest)
    local questType = getQuestType(quest)
    local targetName = getQuestName(quest)
    local eggName = nil

    if questType == "hatchPet" and targetName then
        eggName = getEggForPetName(tostring(targetName))
    elseif targetName and type(EggsModule) == "table" and EggsModule[targetName] then
        eggName = tostring(targetName)
    elseif tostring(questType):lower():find("hatch", 1, true) then
        eggName = getEggForPetRarity(questTypeToRarity(questType))
    end

    eggName = eggName or getBestEggName() or getNearestEggName()
    if not eggName then return false end

    openEgg(eggName, getEggModelByName(eggName))
    return true
end

function claimReadyFarmsForQuest(maxClaims)
    local claimed = 0
    for _, farm in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Farm")) do
        if claimed >= (maxClaims or 3) then break end
        local farmId = farm:GetAttribute("farmId") or farm:GetAttribute("id")
        if farmId then
            local result, err = safeServiceCall(FarmService, "claim", farmId)
            if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then
                claimed = claimed + 1
                task.wait(0.1)
            end
        end
    end
    return claimed
end

function buildQuestBuilding(quest)
    local data = getData() or {}
    local target = tostring(getQuestName(quest) or ""):lower()
    for buildingId, info in pairs(BuildingsList or {}) do
        local display = tostring(type(info) == "table" and (info.name or info.Name) or buildingId):lower()
        local wanted = target == "" or display == target or tostring(buildingId):lower() == target
        local alreadyBuilt = type(data.buildings) == "table" and data.buildings[buildingId]
        if wanted and not alreadyBuilt then
            local result, err = safeServiceCall(BuildingService, "build", buildingId)
            return serviceCallSucceeded(result, err)
        end
    end
    return false
end

function useFirstAuraDiceForQuest()
    local data = getData()
    if not data or type(data.inventory) ~= "table" then return false end
    local auraDice = data.inventory.auraDice or data.inventory.dice or data.inventory.aura
    if type(auraDice) == "table" then
        for itemId, rawItem in pairs(auraDice) do
            local itemName = tostring(itemId)
            local amount = 1
            if itemUtils and itemUtils.getItemFromId then
                local ok, itemObject = pcall(function() return itemUtils.getItemFromId(data, itemId) end)
                if ok and itemObject then
                    pcall(function() itemName = tostring(itemObject:getName()) end)
                    pcall(function() amount = tonumber(itemObject:getAmount()) or amount end)
                end
            elseif type(rawItem) == "table" then
                itemName = tostring(rawItem.nm or rawItem.name or itemId)
                amount = tonumber(rawItem.amount or rawItem.a or rawItem.am) or amount
            elseif type(rawItem) == "number" then
                amount = rawItem
            end

            if amount > 0 then
                local result, err = callFirstQuestMethod(AuraService, { "roll", "rollAura", "useDice" }, itemName)
                if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then return true end
            end
        end
    end

    local result, err = callFirstQuestMethod(AuraService, { "roll", "rollAura" })
    return serviceCallSucceeded(result, err)
end

function craftAnyPetsForQuest(maxCrafts)
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return false end
    local petContainer = (type(data.inventory) == "table" and data.inventory.pet) or data.pets
    if type(petContainer) ~= "table" then return false end

    local petIds = {}
    for petId in pairs(petContainer) do
        table.insert(petIds, petId)
        if #petIds >= 20 then break end
    end
    if #petIds == 0 then return false end

    local result, err = safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", petIds, true)
    return serviceCallSucceeded(result, err)
end

function craftAnyRingForQuest()
    return autoCraftRingsBatch(1, false) > 0
end

function craftAnySmoothieForQuest()
    local selected = firstValue(Library.Flags["SelectedSmoothie"])
    if selected and selected ~= "None" then
        local result = safeServiceCall(RewardService, "craftSmoothie", selected)
        if serviceCallSucceeded(result) then return true end
    end
    for smoothieId in pairs(SmoothiesList or {}) do
        local result, err = safeServiceCall(RewardService, "craftSmoothie", smoothieId)
        if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then return true end
    end
    return false
end

function placeAnyTotemForQuest()
    if placeSelectedTotemIfNeeded() then return true end
    local data = getData()
    if not data or type(data.inventory) ~= "table" then return false end
    local totems = data.inventory.totem or data.inventory.totems
    if type(totems) ~= "table" then return false end

    for itemId in pairs(totems) do
        local result, err = safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", itemId, {
            mapId = getCurrentMapIdForItemUse(),
            use = 1,
        })
        if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then return true end
    end
    return false
end

function claimStarsForQuest()
    local claimed = 0
    for _, star in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("FallingStar")) do
        local result, err = safeServiceCall(FallingStarsService, "claimStar", star.Name)
        if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then
            claimed = claimed + 1
            task.wait(0.05)
        end
    end
    return claimed > 0
end

function runQuestAction(quest, source)
    if type(quest) ~= "table" then return false end
    local questType = getQuestType(quest)
    local lower = tostring(questType):lower()

    if lower == "rebirths" or lower:find("rebirth", 1, true) then
        local best = getBestRebirthIndex()
        if best and best > 0 then
            safeServiceCall(RebirthService, "rebirth", best)
            return true
        end
        return false
    end

    if lower == "hatchpet" or (lower:find("hatch", 1, true) and lower:find("pet", 1, true)) or lower == "openegg" or lower == "openanyegg" or (lower:find("open", 1, true) and lower:find("egg", 1, true)) then
        return openQuestEgg(quest)
    end

    if lower == "building" then
        return buildQuestBuilding(quest)
    end

    if lower:find("tree", 1, true) then
        teleportToSpawnForQuest()
        farmTree(false, getSpawnMapId())
        return true
    end

    if lower:find("ore", 1, true) then
        mineOre(false)
        return true
    end

    if lower:find("potion", 1, true) or lower == "useitem" then
        return useLowestPotionForQuest(quest)
    end

    if lower:find("auradice", 1, true) or lower:find("dice", 1, true) or lower:find("aura", 1, true) then
        return useFirstAuraDiceForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("fruit", 1, true) or lower:find("plant", 1, true) then
        if useInventoryItems({ "fruit" }, 1) > 0 then return true end
        return claimReadyFarmsForQuest(3) > 0
    end

    if lower:find("honey", 1, true) then
        callFirstQuestMethod(HiveService, { "claimHoney", "collectHoney", "claim" })
        return true
    end

    if lower:find("box", 1, true) or lower:find("crate", 1, true) then
        return useInventoryItems({ "box", "crate" }, 1) > 0
    end

    if lower:find("chest", 1, true) then
        claimAllChests()
        claimAllMiniChests()
        return true
    end

    if lower:find("ring", 1, true) then
        return craftAnyRingForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("smoothie", 1, true) then
        return craftAnySmoothieForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("craft", 1, true) then
        if lower:find("golden", 1, true) or lower:find("toxic", 1, true) or lower:find("galaxy", 1, true) or lower:find("pet", 1, true) then
            return craftAnyPetsForQuest(1)
        end
        return craftAnyRingForQuest() or craftAnySmoothieForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("totem", 1, true) then
        return placeAnyTotemForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("playtime", 1, true) then
        claimPlaytimeRewards()
        return true
    end

    if lower:find("star", 1, true) or lower:find("meteor", 1, true) then
        return claimStarsForQuest()
    end

    if lower:find("dungeon", 1, true) then
        return startSelectedDungeon()
    end

    return false
end

function runMapQuestStep()
    local quest, questId, mapData, nextMapId, allComplete = getCurrentMapQuest()
    if allComplete and nextMapId then
        touchMapWall(nextMapId)
        return
    end
    if not quest then return end
    runQuestAction(quest, "map")
end

function runAngelQuestStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local tier = tonumber(data.angelQuestTier) or 1
    local info = AngelQuests and AngelQuests[tier]
    if type(info) ~= "table" or type(info.quest) ~= "table" then return end

    local quest = info.quest
    local progress = tonumber(data.angelQuestProgress) or 0
    if progress >= getQuestRequired(quest) then
        callFirstQuestMethod(QuestService, { "claimAngelQuest" })
        return
    end

    runQuestAction(quest, "angel")
end

function runMinerQuestStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end
    local tier = tonumber(data.minerQuestTier) or 1
    local info = MinerQuests and MinerQuests[tier]
    if type(info) ~= "table" then return end

    local quest = info.quest
    local progress = tonumber(data.minerQuestProgress) or 0

    local function getRequired()
        if type(quest) == "table" then
            return getQuestRequired(quest)
        end
        return tonumber(info.amount) or 1
    end

    if progress >= getRequired() then
        callFirstQuestMethod(QuestService, { "claimMinerQuest" })
        return
    end

    local questType = type(quest) == "table" and getQuestType(quest) or tostring(quest)
    local questName = type(quest) == "table" and (getQuestName(quest) or info.name) or info.name
    local lowerType = tostring(questType):lower()

    if lowerType == "openegg" or (lowerType:find("open") and lowerType:find("egg")) then
        if questName and questName ~= "" then
            safeServiceCall(EggService, "openEgg", questName, 99)
        end
        mineOre(false)
        return
    end

    if lowerType:find("ore") then
        mineOre(false)
        return
    end

    if type(quest) == "table" then
        runQuestAction(quest, "miner")
    end
end

function getQuestListCache()
    if QuestListCache then return QuestListCache end
    QuestListCache = {}
    if not SharedList then return QuestListCache end

    for _, inst in ipairs(SharedList:GetDescendants()) do
        if inst:IsA("ModuleScript") and inst.Name:lower():find("quest", 1, true) then
            local ok, result = pcall(require, inst)
            if ok and type(result) == "table" then
                table.insert(QuestListCache, result)
            end
        end
    end

    return QuestListCache
end

function resolveQuestDefinition(storedQuest)
    if type(storedQuest) ~= "table" then return nil end
    if type(storedQuest.quest) == "table" then return storedQuest.quest end
    if type(storedQuest.quest) == "string" then return storedQuest end

    local difficulty = storedQuest.questDifficulty or storedQuest.difficulty or storedQuest.Difficulty
    local questId = storedQuest.questId or storedQuest.id or storedQuest.Id
    if questId == nil then return nil end

    for _, questList in ipairs(getQuestListCache()) do
        local entry = nil
        if difficulty ~= nil and type(questList[difficulty]) == "table" then
            entry = questList[difficulty][questId] or questList[difficulty][tostring(questId)]
        end
        entry = entry or questList[questId] or questList[tostring(questId)]
        if type(entry) == "table" then
            if type(entry.quest) == "table" then return entry.quest end
            if type(entry.quest) == "string" then return entry end
        end
    end

    return nil
end

function runGenericEventQuestStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return end

    for dataKey, questTable in pairs(data) do
        local keyLower = tostring(dataKey):lower()
        local isEventQuestTable = keyLower:find("quest", 1, true)
            and keyLower ~= "mapquests"
            and keyLower ~= "classicquests"
            and type(questTable) == "table"

        if isEventQuestTable then
            for questId, storedQuest in pairs(questTable) do
                if type(storedQuest) == "table" and not storedQuest.claimed and not storedQuest.isPremium then
                    local quest = resolveQuestDefinition(storedQuest)
                    if quest then
                        local progress = getQuestProgress(questTable, questId, storedQuest)
                        if progress < getQuestRequired(quest) then
                            runQuestAction(quest, "event")
                            return
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end


-- Season helpers

function getCurrentSeasonNumber()
    return tonumber(Variables and Variables.season) or CurrentSeasonNumber or 9
end

function getSeasonDataKey(suffix)
    return "season" .. tostring(getCurrentSeasonNumber()) .. tostring(suffix or "")
end

function getSortedSeasonTierIds()
    local ids = {}
    for tierId in pairs(CurrentSeasonTiers or {}) do
        table.insert(ids, tierId)
    end
    table.sort(ids, function(a, b)
        return (tonumber(a) or 0) < (tonumber(b) or 0)
    end)
    return ids
end

function getCurrentSeasonPassLevel(data)
    data = data or getData() or {}
    if Util and Util.seasonUtils and type(Util.seasonUtils.getPassLevel) == "function" then
        local ok, level = pcall(function()
            return Util.seasonUtils.getPassLevel(data)
        end)
        if ok then return tonumber(level) or 0 end
    end
    return 0
end

function getCurrentSeasonRestartPrice(data)
    data = data or getData() or {}
    if Util and Util.seasonUtils and type(Util.seasonUtils.getRestartPrice) == "function" then
        local ok, price = pcall(function()
            return Util.seasonUtils.getRestartPrice(data)
        end)
        if ok then return tonumber(price) or math.huge end
    end
    return math.huge
end

function countSeasonClaimedRewards(data)
    data = data or getData() or {}
    local claimed = data[getSeasonDataKey("PassClaimed")]
    if type(claimed) ~= "table" then return 0 end

    local count = 0
    for _, value in pairs(claimed) do
        if value then count = count + 1 end
    end
    return count
end

function claimCurrentSeasonPassRewardsStep(maxClaims)
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return 0 end

    local season = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
    local level = getCurrentSeasonPassLevel(data)
    local claimedTable = data[getSeasonDataKey("PassClaimed")]
    if type(claimedTable) ~= "table" then return 0 end

    local premium = data[getSeasonDataKey("PassPremium")] == true
    local claimed = 0
    local limit = tonumber(maxClaims) or 10

    for _, tierId in ipairs(getSortedSeasonTierIds()) do
        local tierNumber = tonumber(tierId) or tierId
        if (tonumber(tierNumber) or 0) <= level then
            for passType = 1, (premium and 2 or 1) do
                local claimKey = tostring(passType) .. tostring(tierId)
                if not claimedTable[claimKey] then
                    local result, err = safeServiceCall(SeasonService, "claimTier", tierNumber, passType, true)
                    if serviceCallSucceeded(result, err) then
                        claimedTable[claimKey] = true
                        claimed = claimed + 1
                        task.wait(0.08)
                        if claimed >= limit then return claimed end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    return claimed
end

function resetCurrentSeasonPassStep()
    local data = getData()
    if not data then return false end

    local premium = data[getSeasonDataKey("PassPremium")] == true
    local seasonTierIds = getSortedSeasonTierIds()
    local requiredClaims = #seasonTierIds * (premium and 2 or 1)
    if requiredClaims <= 0 then return false end
    if countSeasonClaimedRewards(data) < requiredClaims then return false end

    local restarts = tonumber(data[getSeasonDataKey("PassRestarts")]) or 0
    local restartLimit = tonumber(Variables and Variables.seasonRestartLimit) or 100
    if restarts >= restartLimit then return false end

    local price = getCurrentSeasonRestartPrice(data)
    if price ~= math.huge and getCurrency(data, "gems") < price then return false end

    local result, err = safeServiceCall(SeasonService, "resetPass", true)
    return serviceCallSucceeded(result, err)
end

function runCurrentSeasonQuestStep()
    if SeasonQuestState.busying and tick() < SeasonQuestState.busyUntil then return false end
    SeasonQuestState.busying = true
    SeasonQuestState.busyUntil = tick() + 6
    local data = getData()
    if not data then SeasonQuestState.busying = false return false end

    local season = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
    local seasonKey = "season" .. tostring(season) .. "Quests"
    local questTable = data[seasonKey]
    if type(questTable) ~= "table" then SeasonQuestState.busying = false return false end

    local mod = getQuestModule()
    if not mod then SeasonQuestState.busying = false return false end

    -- Build active quests map
    local activeQuests = {}
    for slotIndex, questSlot in pairs(questTable) do
        local difficulty = questSlot.questDifficulty or "unknown"
        local questId = questSlot.questId
        local progress = questSlot.progress or 0
        local questSet = mod[difficulty]
        local questInfo = questSet and questSet[questId]
        if questInfo and questInfo.quest then
            local q = questInfo.quest
            local questType = q.quest
            local required = q.amount or 0
            if questType and progress < required then
                activeQuests[questType] = {
                    slotIndex = slotIndex, difficulty = difficulty,
                    progress = progress, required = required,
                    questInfo = questInfo, questData = q,
                }
            end
        end
    end

    if not next(activeQuests) then return false end

    -- Categorize quests
    local selectedQuests = SeasonQuestState.selectedQuests or {}
    local useSelected = #selectedQuests > 0
    local eggQuest, mythicalEternalQuest = nil, nil
    local meteorQuest, treeQuest, fishQuest, oreQuest = nil, nil, nil, nil
    local otherQuests = {}

    for questType, info in pairs(activeQuests) do
        local skipQuest = false
        if useSelected then
            local found = false
            for _, sq in ipairs(selectedQuests) do
                if sq == questType then found = true break end
            end
            if not found then skipQuest = true end
        end
        if not skipQuest then
            if questType == "hatchMythicalPet" or questType == "hatchEternalPet" then
                mythicalEternalQuest = info
                eggQuest = nil
            elseif questType == "openAnyEgg" or questType == "hatchEpicPet" or questType == "hatchLegendaryPet" then
                if not mythicalEternalQuest then eggQuest = info end
            elseif questType == "destroyMeteor" then
                meteorQuest = info
            elseif questType == "destroyTree" or questType == "destroyAnyTree" then
                treeQuest = info
            elseif questType:find("catchFish") or questType == "catchAnyFish" or questType == "catchFishRarity" then
                fishQuest = info
            elseif questType:find("destroyOre") or questType == "destroyAnyOre" then
                oreQuest = info
            else
                table.insert(otherQuests, {type = questType, data = info})
            end
        end
    end

    local nextCheckTime = tick() + 4.5
    local threads = {}

    -- Egg quest
    if eggQuest and _G.CurrentResourceQuest ~= "tree" then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                local eggName = resolveBestEgg(
                    SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg,
                    SeasonQuestState.eggOptions,
                    SeasonQuestState.displayToEggName
                ) or getBestEggName() or getNearestEggName()
                if eggName then
                    safeServiceCall(EggService, "openEgg", eggName, 999)
                end
                task.wait(_G.SmartHatchDelay or 2.1)
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Mythical/Eternal egg quest
    if mythicalEternalQuest and _G.CurrentResourceQuest ~= "tree" then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                local eggName = resolveBestEgg(
                    SeasonQuestState.selectedMythicalEternalEgg,
                    SeasonQuestState.eggOptions,
                    SeasonQuestState.displayToEggName
                ) or getBestEggName() or getNearestEggName()
                if eggName then
                    safeServiceCall(EggService, "openEgg", eggName, 999)
                end
                task.wait(_G.SmartHatchDelay or 2.1)
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Meteor quest
    if meteorQuest then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                for _, meteor in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Meteor")) do
                    if meteor and meteor:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) then
                        local meteorId = meteor:GetAttribute("meteorId")
                        if meteorId then
                            local es = safeGetKnitService("EventService")
                            if es and es.damageMeteor and es.damageMeteor._re then
                                pcall(function() es.damageMeteor._re:FireServer(meteorId) end)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                task.wait(3)
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Resource quest coordination
    if not _G.CurrentResourceQuest then
        local choices = {}
        if treeQuest then table.insert(choices, "tree") end
        if fishQuest then table.insert(choices, "fish") end
        if oreQuest then table.insert(choices, "ore") end
        _G.CurrentResourceQuest = #choices > 0 and choices[math.random(#choices)] or nil
    end
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "tree" and not treeQuest then _G.CurrentResourceQuest = nil end
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "fish" and not fishQuest then _G.CurrentResourceQuest = nil end
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "ore" and not oreQuest then _G.CurrentResourceQuest = nil end

    -- Tree quest
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "tree" and treeQuest then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            local treesToCut = {"spawn", "desert", "nuclear"}
            while tick() < nextCheckTime and _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "tree" and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                pcall(function()
                    local pd = getData()
                    if not pd then return end

                    -- Equip axe if needed
                    if not pd.isAxeEquipped and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.exclusive then
                        local axeIdx, curIdx
                        for i, itemData in pairs(pd.inventory.exclusive) do
                            local itemName = type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name or "") or ""
                            if itemName:lower():find("axe") and not itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") then axeIdx = i end
                            if pd.isFishingRodEquipped and (itemName:lower():find("fishingrod") or itemName:lower():find("rod")) then curIdx = i end
                            if pd.isPickaxeEquipped and itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") and not curIdx then curIdx = i end
                        end
                        if curIdx then pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", curIdx, {use = 1}) end) task.wait(0.5) end
                        if axeIdx then pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", axeIdx, {use = 1}) end) task.wait(0.5) end
                    end

                    -- Find weakest tree
                    local hrp = getHRP()
                    if not hrp then return end
                    local playerPos = hrp.Position
                    local lowestHP, targetTree, targetGroup, targetId = math.huge, nil, nil, nil
                    for _, groupId in ipairs(treesToCut) do
                        local activeTrees = getActiveTreesInGroup(groupId, pd)
                        for _, treeInfo in ipairs(activeTrees) do
                            if treeInfo.hp > 0 and treeInfo.hp < lowestHP then
                                lowestHP = treeInfo.hp
                                targetTree = treeInfo.instance
                                targetGroup = groupId
                                targetId = treeInfo.treeId
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    -- Teleport to weakest tree
                    if targetTree then
                        local model = targetTree:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Model")
                        if model then
                            hrp.CFrame = model:GetPivot() + Vector3.new(2, 1, 0)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end

                    -- Find closest tagged tree and damage
                    local closestTree, closestDist = nil, math.huge
                    for _, tree in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Tree")) do
                        local model = tree:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Model")
                        if model then
                            local pp = model.PrimaryPart or model:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                            if pp then
                                local dist = (pp.Position - playerPos).Magnitude
                                if dist < closestDist then closestDist = dist closestTree = tree end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if closestTree and TreeController then
                        pcall(function()
                            local origGetRay = TreeController.getRay
                            TreeController.getRay = function(_, _, _) return true end
                            local origGetTree = TreeController.getTreeFromRayResult
                            TreeController.getTreeFromRayResult = function(_, _) return closestTree end
                            TreeController:sendRayFromInput(0, 0)
                            TreeController.getRay = origGetRay
                            TreeController.getTreeFromRayResult = origGetTree
                        end)
                        local treeGroupId = closestTree:GetAttribute("groupId")
                        local treeId = closestTree:GetAttribute("treeId")
                        local lumberId
                        if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.exclusive then
                            for i, itemData in pairs(pd.inventory.exclusive) do
                                local itemName = type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name or "") or ""
                                if itemName:lower():find("axe") and not itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") then lumberId = i break end
                            end
                        end
                        if treeGroupId and treeId and lumberId and TreeService and TreeService.damage2 then
                            TreeService.damage2:Fire(treeGroupId, treeId, lumberId)
                        end
                    end
                end)
                task.wait(1)
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Fish quest
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "fish" and fishQuest then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            pcall(function()
                local pd = getData()
                if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.exclusive then
                    local rodIdx, curIdx
                    for i, itemData in pairs(pd.inventory.exclusive) do
                        local itemName = type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name or "") or ""
                        if itemName:lower():find("fishingrod") or itemName:lower():find("rod") then rodIdx = i end
                        if not pd.isFishingRodEquipped then
                            if pd.isAxeEquipped and itemName:lower():find("axe") and not itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") then curIdx = i end
                            if pd.isPickaxeEquipped and itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") and not curIdx then curIdx = i end
                        end
                    end
                    if curIdx then pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", curIdx, {use = 1}) end) task.wait(0.5) end
                    if rodIdx and not pd.isFishingRodEquipped then
                        pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", rodIdx, {use = 1}) end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
            end)
            while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                local fs = safeGetKnitService("FishingService")
                if fs then
                    if fs.fishRequest and fs.fishRequest._re then pcall(function() fs.fishRequest._re:FireServer() end) end
                    task.wait(0.15)
                    if fs.fishCatched and fs.fishCatched._re then pcall(function() fs.fishCatched._re:FireServer() end) end
                    task.wait(0.15)
                end
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Ore quest
    if _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "ore" and oreQuest then
        table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
            -- Equip pickaxe
            pcall(function()
                local pd = getData()
                if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.exclusive then
                    local pickIdx, curIdx
                    for i, itemData in pairs(pd.inventory.exclusive) do
                        local itemName = type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name or "") or ""
                        if itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") then pickIdx = i end
                        if not pd.isPickaxeEquipped then
                            if pd.isFishingRodEquipped and (itemName:lower():find("fishingrod") or itemName:lower():find("rod")) then curIdx = i end
                            if pd.isAxeEquipped and itemName:lower():find("axe") and not itemName:lower():find("pickaxe") and not curIdx then curIdx = i end
                        end
                    end
                    if curIdx then pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", curIdx, {use = 1}) end) task.wait(0.5) end
                    if pickIdx and not pd.isPickaxeEquipped then
                        pcall(function() safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", pickIdx, {use = 1}) end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
            end)

            -- Teleport to Space Mine every 20s
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] and _G.CurrentResourceQuest == "ore" do
                    pcall(function()
                        local Maps = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Maps" }, "Maps") or {}
                        for _, mapData in pairs(Maps) do
                            if mapData.machines then
                                for _, machine in pairs(mapData.machines) do
                                    if machine.name == "Space Mine" and machine.teleport then
                                        local hrp = getHRP()
                                        if hrp then
                                            pcall(function() client:RequestStreamAroundAsync(machine.teleport.p, 5) end)
                                            task.wait(0.5)
                                            hrp:PivotTo(machine.teleport)
                                        end
                                        return
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(20)
                end
            end))

            -- Determine target ore
            local Ores = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Mine", "Ores" }, "Mine.Ores") or {}
            local matchAnyOre = oreQuest.type == "destroyAnyOre"
            local targetOreId
            if not matchAnyOre then
                local currentSeason = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
                local seasonObj = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.List:FindFirstChild("Season" .. tostring(currentSeason))
                if seasonObj then
                    if seasonObj:IsA("Folder") then
                        local p = seasonObj:FindFirstChild("Quests")
                        if p and p:IsA("ModuleScript") then seasonObj = p else seasonObj = seasonObj:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ModuleScript") end
                    end
                    if seasonObj and seasonObj:IsA("ModuleScript") then
                        local SeasonModule = require(seasonObj)
                        local QM = SeasonModule.Quests or SeasonModule
                        local pd = getData()
                        local sqData = pd and pd[("season%dQuests"):format(currentSeason)] or {}
                        for _, qSlot in pairs(sqData) do
                            local qs = QM[qSlot.questDifficulty]
                            local qi = qs and qs[qSlot.questId]
                            if qi and qi.quest and (qi.quest.quest == "destroyOre" or (qi.quest.quest or ""):find("destroyOre")) then
                                targetOreId = qi.quest.name
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            local pickDamage = getPickaxeDamage()
            local OreService = safeGetKnitService("OreService")

            while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                local pd = getData()
                if not pd or not pd.ores then
                    task.wait(0.25)
                elseif matchAnyOre then
                    local lowestHP, tRoom, tId = math.huge, nil, nil
                    for _, ore in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Ore")) do
                        local roomId = ore:GetAttribute("roomId")
                        local id = ore:GetAttribute("id")
                        if roomId and id and pd.ores[roomId] and pd.ores[roomId][id] then
                            local info = pd.ores[roomId][id]
                            local oreData = Ores[info.oreId]
                            if oreData then
                                local hitsNeeded = math.ceil(oreData.hp / pickDamage)
                                local remaining = oreData.hp - (info.damage or 0)
                                if hitsNeeded <= 75 and remaining > 0 and remaining < lowestHP then
                                    lowestHP = remaining tRoom = roomId tId = id
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if tRoom and tId then
                        local hrp = getHRP()
                        if hrp then
                            local orePart = (function() for _, o in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Ore")) do if o:GetAttribute("roomId") == tRoom and o:GetAttribute("id") == tId then return o.PrimaryPart or o:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") end end end)()
                            if orePart then hrp.CFrame = orePart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0) end
                        end
                        if OreService and OreService.damage and OreService.damage._re then
                            pcall(function() OreService.damage._re:FireServer(tRoom, tId) end)
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(0.25)
                elseif targetOreId then
                    local foundRoom, foundId
                    for _, ore in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Ore")) do
                        local roomId = ore:GetAttribute("roomId")
                        local id = ore:GetAttribute("id")
                        if roomId and id and pd.ores[roomId] and pd.ores[roomId][id] then
                            local info = pd.ores[roomId][id]
                            local oreData = Ores[info.oreId]
                            if oreData and info.oreId == targetOreId then
                                local hitsNeeded = math.ceil(oreData.hp / pickDamage)
                                local remaining = oreData.hp - (info.damage or 0)
                                if hitsNeeded <= 75 and remaining > 0 then foundRoom = roomId foundId = id break end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if foundRoom and foundId then
                        if OreService and OreService.damage and OreService.damage._re then
                            pcall(function() OreService.damage._re:FireServer(foundRoom, foundId) end)
                        end
                        task.wait(0.25)
                    else
                        local bestRoom = findBestRoomForOre(targetOreId, pickDamage)
                        local wRoom, wId
                        for _, ore in ipairs(CollectionService:GetTagged("Ore")) do
                            local roomId = ore:GetAttribute("roomId")
                            local id = ore:GetAttribute("id")
                            if roomId == bestRoom and id and pd.ores[roomId] and pd.ores[roomId][id] then
                                local info = pd.ores[roomId][id]
                                local oreData = Ores[info.oreId]
                                if oreData then
                                    local hitsNeeded = math.ceil(oreData.hp / pickDamage)
                                    local remaining = oreData.hp - (info.damage or 0)
                                    if hitsNeeded <= 75 and remaining > 0 then wRoom = roomId wId = id break end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        if wRoom and wId and OreService and OreService.damage and OreService.damage._re then
                            pcall(function() OreService.damage._re:FireServer(wRoom, wId) end)
                        end
                        task.wait(0.25)
                    end
                end
            end
        end))
    end

    -- Other quest type handlers
    for _, quest in ipairs(otherQuests) do
        local qt = quest.type
        local qd = quest.data

        if qt == "usePotions" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    local pd = getData()
                    if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.potion then
                        local bestId, bestAm
                        for id, d in pairs(pd.inventory.potion) do
                            if d.am and d.am > (bestAm or 0) then bestAm = d.am bestId = id end
                        end
                        if bestId then
                            local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                            safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", bestId, {use = math.min(remaining, bestAm)})
                            task.wait(5)
                        else break end
                    else break end
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "craftSmoothie" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local Smoothies = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Items", "Smoothies" }, "Items.Smoothies") or {}
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory then return end
                        local resourceAmounts = {}
                        for cat, items in pairs(pd.inventory) do
                            if type(items) == "table" then
                                for _, itemData in pairs(items) do
                                    local name = (type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.nm or itemData.name)) or "Unknown"
                                    local amt = (type(itemData) == "table" and (itemData.am or itemData.amount)) or 0
                                    resourceAmounts[name] = (resourceAmounts[name] or 0) + amt
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        local bestSmoothie, maxCraftable
                        for sid, sData in pairs(Smoothies) do
                            local sName = sData.name or tostring(sid)
                            if sName ~= "Chaos Smoothie" and sName ~= "Insane Smoothie" then
                                local canCraft = math.huge
                                if sData.required then
                                    for _, req in ipairs(sData.required) do
                                        local rName = type(req) == "table" and (req.nm or req.name or "Unknown") or tostring(req)
                                        local rAmt = type(req) == "table" and (req.am or req.amount or 0) or 1
                                        local have = resourceAmounts[rName] or 0
                                        local possible = rAmt > 0 and math.floor(have / rAmt) or 0
                                        canCraft = math.min(canCraft, possible)
                                    end
                                end
                                if canCraft > (maxCraftable or 0) then maxCraftable = canCraft bestSmoothie = sid end
                            end
                        end
                        if bestSmoothie and (maxCraftable or 0) > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "craftSmoothie", bestSmoothie, math.min(maxCraftable, qd.required - qd.progress))
                            task.wait(5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(3)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "craftUltraPotions" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local MagicPot = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "MagicPot" }, "MagicPot") or {}
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory then return end
                        local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                        if remaining <= 0 then return end
                        local bestIdx, maxCraftable
                        for idx = 10, 12 do
                            local potData = MagicPot[idx]
                            if potData and potData.required then
                                local canCraft = math.huge
                                for _, req in ipairs(potData.required) do
                                    local reqItem = type(req) == "table" and req
                                    if reqItem then
                                        local rName = (reqItem.nm or reqItem.name or "")
                                        local rAmt = (reqItem.am or reqItem.amount or 0)
                                        local have = 0
                                        if pd.inventory.potion then
                                            for _, d in pairs(pd.inventory.potion) do
                                                if (d.nm or d.name) == rName then have = (d.am or 0) break end
                                            end
                                        end
                                        canCraft = math.min(canCraft, rAmt > 0 and math.floor(have / rAmt) or 0)
                                    end
                                end
                                if canCraft > (maxCraftable or 0) then maxCraftable = canCraft bestIdx = idx end
                            end
                        end
                        if bestIdx and (maxCraftable or 0) > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "magicPot", bestIdx, math.min(maxCraftable, remaining))
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(5.25)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "useMegaPotions" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    local pd = getData()
                    if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.potion then
                        local bestId, bestAm
                        for id, d in pairs(pd.inventory.potion) do
                            local name = (d.nm or tostring(id)):lower()
                            if name:find("mega") and (d.am or 0) > (bestAm or 0) then bestAm = d.am bestId = id end
                        end
                        if bestId then
                            safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", bestId, {use = math.min(qd.required - qd.progress, bestAm)})
                            task.wait(5)
                        else break end
                    else break end
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "craftMegaPotions" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local MagicPot = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "MagicPot" }, "MagicPot") or {}
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory then return end
                        local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                        if remaining <= 0 then return end
                        local bestIdx, maxCraftable
                        for idx = 4, 9 do
                            local potData = MagicPot[idx]
                            if potData and potData.required then
                                local canCraft = math.huge
                                for _, req in ipairs(potData.required) do
                                    local reqItem = type(req) == "table" and req
                                    if reqItem then
                                        local rName = (reqItem.nm or reqItem.name or "")
                                        local rAmt = (reqItem.am or reqItem.amount or 0)
                                        local have = 0
                                        if pd.inventory.potion then
                                            for _, d in pairs(pd.inventory.potion) do
                                                if (d.nm or d.name) == rName then have = (d.am or 0) break end
                                            end
                                        end
                                        canCraft = math.min(canCraft, rAmt > 0 and math.floor(have / rAmt) or 0)
                                    end
                                end
                                if canCraft > (maxCraftable or 0) then maxCraftable = canCraft bestIdx = idx end
                            end
                        end
                        if bestIdx and (maxCraftable or 0) > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "magicPot", bestIdx, math.min(maxCraftable, remaining))
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(5.25)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "useAuraDice" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                local ad = SeasonQuestState.selectedAuraDice
                if ad and next(ad) then
                    local AuraDices = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Items", "AuraDices" }, "Items.AuraDices") or {}
                    while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                        for diceName, isSel in pairs(ad) do
                            if isSel then
                                for diceId, diceData in pairs(AuraDices) do
                                    if diceData.name == diceName then
                                        safeServiceCall(AuraService, "roll", diceId)
                                        task.wait(0.5)
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "collectPlaytimeRewards" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local holder = client:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui") and client.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("MainUI") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI:FindFirstChild("Menus") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI.Menus:FindFirstChild("RewardsFrame") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI.Menus.RewardsFrame:FindFirstChild("Main") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI.Menus.RewardsFrame.Main:FindFirstChild("Displays") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI.Menus.RewardsFrame.Main.Displays:FindFirstChild("Playtime") and client.PlayerGui.MainUI.Menus.RewardsFrame.Main.Displays.Playtime:FindFirstChild("Holder")
                        if holder then
                            for _, rf in ipairs(holder:GetChildren()) do
                                if rf:IsA("Frame") then
                                    local rid = tonumber(rf.Name)
                                    local timer = rf:FindFirstChild("Main", true) and rf.Main:FindFirstChild("Timer")
                                    if timer and timer.Text == "Claim" and rid then
                                        safeServiceCall(RewardService, "claimPlaytimeReward", rid)
                                        task.wait(1)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(10)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "ancientSpin" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    safeServiceCall(RewardService, "ancientWheelSpin")
                    task.wait(2)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "useGoldenFruit" or qt == "useFruit" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    local pd = getData()
                    if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.fruit then
                        local found = false
                        for fid, fd in pairs(pd.inventory.fruit) do
                            if (qt ~= "useGoldenFruit" or ((fd.nm or ""):lower():find("golden"))) and (fd.am or 0) > 0 then
                                safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", fid, {use = math.min(qd.required - qd.progress, fd.am)})
                                task.wait(5)
                                found = true
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        if not found then break end
                    else break end
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "useCircusTickets" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function() safeServiceCall(RewardService, "playCircusMinigame", 10, "normal") end)
                    task.wait(2.75)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "openMeteoriteFragment" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory or not pd.inventory.mapItem then return end
                        local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                        if remaining <= 0 then return end
                        local LunarForgeList = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "LunarForge" }, "LunarForge") or {}
                        local bestForgeId, bestAmt
                        for _, fd in pairs(pd.inventory.mapItem) do
                            local item = type(fd) == "table" and fd
                            if item then
                                local itemName = item.nm or item.name or ""
                                local amt = item.am or item.amount or 0
                                for forgeId, forgeData in pairs(LunarForgeList) do
                                    local forgeItem = forgeData.item
                                    local forgeName = type(forgeItem) == "table" and (forgeItem.nm or forgeItem.name or "")
                                    if forgeName ~= "" and forgeName == itemName and amt > (bestAmt or 0) then
                                        bestAmt = amt bestForgeId = forgeId
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        if bestForgeId and (bestAmt or 0) > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "lunarForge", bestForgeId, math.min(remaining, bestAmt))
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(5)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "playDungeons" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function() safeServiceCall(DungeonService, "startDungeon", 1) end)
                    task.wait(3)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "buyDungeonShop" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        for slot = 1, 3 do
                            safeServiceCall(DungeonService, "buyShop", slot)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(5)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "craftGolden" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                local targetRarity
                do
                    local currentSeason = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
                    local seasonObj = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.List:FindFirstChild("Season" .. tostring(currentSeason))
                    if seasonObj then
                        if seasonObj:IsA("Folder") then
                            local p = seasonObj:FindFirstChild("Quests")
                            if p and p:IsA("ModuleScript") then seasonObj = p else seasonObj = seasonObj:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ModuleScript") end
                        end
                        if seasonObj and seasonObj:IsA("ModuleScript") then
                            local SM = require(seasonObj)
                            local QM = SM.Quests or SM
                            local pd = getData()
                            local sq = pd and pd[("season%dQuests"):format(currentSeason)] or {}
                            for _, qSlot in pairs(sq) do
                                local qs = QM[qSlot.questDifficulty]
                                local qi = qs and qs[qSlot.questId]
                                if qi and qi.quest and qi.quest.quest == "craftGolden" then targetRarity = qi.quest.name break end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory or not pd.inventory.pet then return end
                        local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                        if remaining <= 0 then return end
                        local PetDefinitions = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Pets" }, "Pets.Pets") or {}
                        local bestId, bestScore
                        for petId, raw in pairs(pd.inventory.pet) do
                            local petDef = PetDefinitions[raw.nm or raw.name or ""]
                            local tier = raw.t or raw.tier or 1
                            local rarity = petDef and petDef.rarity or "Unknown"
                            if tier == 1 and (not targetRarity or rarity == targetRarity) then
                                local canMake = math.floor((raw.am or 0) / 5)
                                if canMake > (bestScore or 0) then bestScore = canMake bestId = petId end
                            end
                        end
                        if bestId and (bestScore or 0) > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = bestId}, false, math.min(bestScore, remaining))
                            task.wait(1)
                        elseif not eggQuest and not mythicalEternalQuest then
                            local eggToUse = (targetRarity == "Mythical" or targetRarity == "Eternal") and
                                (SeasonQuestState.selectedMythicalEternalEgg or SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg) or SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg
                            local eggName = resolveBestEgg(eggToUse, SeasonQuestState.eggOptions, SeasonQuestState.displayToEggName) or getBestEggName()
                            if eggName then
                                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                                    safeServiceCall(EggService, "openEgg", eggName, 999)
                                    task.wait(_G.SmartHatchDelay or 2.1)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(2)
                end
            end))

        elseif qt == "craftToxic" or qt == "craftGalaxy" or qt == "craftAnyGoldenPets" or qt == "craftAnyToxicPets" or qt == "craftAnyGalaxyPets" then
            table.insert(threads, task.spawn(function()
                local targetRarity
                local maxTier = (qt == "craftGalaxy" or qt == "craftAnyGalaxyPets") and 3 or (qt == "craftToxic" or qt == "craftAnyToxicPets") and 2 or 1
                if qt == "craftToxic" or qt == "craftGalaxy" then
                    local currentSeason = getCurrentSeasonNumber()
                    local seasonObj = ReplicatedStorage.Shared.List:FindFirstChild("Season" .. tostring(currentSeason))
                    if seasonObj then
                        if seasonObj:IsA("Folder") then
                            local p = seasonObj:FindFirstChild("Quests")
                            if p and p:IsA("ModuleScript") then seasonObj = p else seasonObj = seasonObj:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ModuleScript") end
                        end
                        if seasonObj and seasonObj:IsA("ModuleScript") then
                            local SM = require(seasonObj)
                            local QM = SM.Quests or SM
                            local pd = getData()
                            local sq = pd and pd[("season%dQuests"):format(currentSeason)] or {}
                            for _, qSlot in pairs(sq) do
                                local qs = QM[qSlot.questDifficulty]
                                local qi = qs and qs[qSlot.questId]
                                if qi and qi.quest and (qi.quest.quest == qt) then targetRarity = qi.quest.name break end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                    pcall(function()
                        local pd = getData()
                        if not pd or not pd.inventory or not pd.inventory.pet then return end
                        local remaining = qd.required - qd.progress
                        if remaining <= 0 then return end
                        local PetDefinitions = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Pets", "Pets" }, "Pets.Pets") or {}

                        -- Group pets by name and tier
                        local petsByName = {}
                        for petId, raw in pairs(pd.inventory.pet) do
                            local petName = raw.nm or raw.name or tostring(petId)
                            local tierNum = raw.t or raw.tier or 1
                            local petDef = PetDefinitions[petName]
                            local rarity = petDef and petDef.rarity or "Unknown"
                            if not targetRarity or rarity == targetRarity then
                                petsByName[petName] = petsByName[petName] or {}
                                petsByName[petName][tierNum] = petsByName[petName][tierNum] or {ids = {}, total = 0}
                                table.insert(petsByName[petName][tierNum].ids, {id = petId, count = raw.am or 0})
                                petsByName[petName][tierNum].total = petsByName[petName][tierNum].total + (raw.am or 0)
                            end
                        end

                        -- Calculate max crafts per pet
                        local bestPet, bestScore
                        for pName, tiers in pairs(petsByName) do
                            local function getTotal(t) return (tiers[t] and tiers[t].total) or 0 end
                            local n = getTotal(1)
                            local g = getTotal(2)
                            local tx = getTotal(3)
                            local totalG = g + math.floor(n / 5)
                            local totalTx = tx + math.floor(totalG / 5)
                            local score = maxTier == 3 and math.floor(totalTx / 5) or maxTier == 2 and math.floor(totalG / 5) or math.floor(n / 5)
                            if score > (bestScore or 0) then bestScore = score bestPet = pName end
                        end

                        if bestPet and (bestScore or 0) > 0 then
                            local tiers = petsByName[bestPet]
                            local toCraft = math.min(bestScore, remaining)

                            -- Step 1: craft normals -> goldens
                            local goldensNeeded = toCraft * 5
                            if maxTier >= 2 and (tiers[2] and tiers[2].total or 0) < goldensNeeded then
                                local need = goldensNeeded - (tiers[2] and tiers[2].total or 0)
                                local normalsNeeded = need * 5
                                if tiers[1] and tiers[1].total >= normalsNeeded then
                                    for _, nd in ipairs(tiers[1].ids) do
                                        if need <= 0 then break end
                                        local canMake = math.floor(nd.count / 5)
                                        local toMake = math.min(canMake, need)
                                        if toMake > 0 then
                                            safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = nd.id}, false, toMake)
                                            need = need - toMake
                                            task.wait(1)
                                        end
                                    end
                                    pd = getData()
                                end
                            end

                            -- Step 2: craft goldens -> toxics
                            local toxicsNeeded = toCraft * 5
                            if maxTier >= 3 and (tiers[3] and tiers[3].total or 0) < toxicsNeeded then
                                pd = getData()
                                local need = toxicsNeeded - (tiers[3] and tiers[3].total or 0)
                                if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.pet then
                                    for petId, raw in pairs(pd.inventory.pet) do
                                        if need <= 0 then break end
                                        local pName = raw.nm or raw.name or ""
                                        local tierNum = raw.t or raw.tier or 1
                                        if pName == bestPet and tierNum == 2 then
                                            local canMake = math.floor((raw.am or 0) / 5)
                                            local toMake = math.min(canMake, need)
                                            if toMake > 0 then
                                                safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = petId}, false, toMake)
                                                need = need - toMake
                                                task.wait(1)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            -- Step 3: craft toxics -> galaxies
                            if maxTier >= 3 then
                                pd = getData()
                                local crafted = 0
                                if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.pet then
                                    for petId, raw in pairs(pd.inventory.pet) do
                                        if crafted >= toCraft then break end
                                        local pName = raw.nm or raw.name or ""
                                        local tierNum = raw.t or raw.tier or 1
                                        if pName == bestPet and tierNum == 3 then
                                            local canMake = math.floor((raw.am or 0) / 5)
                                            local toMake = math.min(canMake, toCraft - crafted)
                                            if toMake > 0 then
                                                safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = petId}, false, toMake)
                                                crafted = crafted + toMake
                                                task.wait(1)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            -- Step 2 (for tier-2 max): craft goldens -> toxics
                            elseif maxTier == 2 then
                                pd = getData()
                                local crafted = 0
                                if pd and pd.inventory and pd.inventory.pet then
                                    for petId, raw in pairs(pd.inventory.pet) do
                                        if crafted >= toCraft then break end
                                        local pName = raw.nm or raw.name or ""
                                        local tierNum = raw.t or raw.tier or 1
                                        if pName == bestPet and tierNum == 2 then
                                            local canMake = math.floor((raw.am or 0) / 5)
                                            local toMake = math.min(canMake, toCraft - crafted)
                                            if toMake > 0 then
                                                safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = petId}, false, toMake)
                                                crafted = crafted + toMake
                                                task.wait(1)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            else
                                -- maxTier == 1: craft normals -> goldens
                                local crafted = 0
                                for _, nd in ipairs(tiers[1] and tiers[1].ids or {}) do
                                    if crafted >= toCraft then break end
                                    local canMake = math.floor(nd.count / 5)
                                    local toMake = math.min(canMake, toCraft - crafted)
                                    if toMake > 0 then
                                        safeServiceCall(PetService, "craft", {[1] = nd.id}, false, toMake)
                                        crafted = crafted + toMake
                                        task.wait(1)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        elseif not eggQuest and not mythicalEternalQuest then
                            local eggName = resolveBestEgg(SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg, SeasonQuestState.eggOptions, SeasonQuestState.displayToEggName) or getBestEggName()
                            if eggName then
                                while tick() < nextCheckTime and Library.Flags["AutoSeasonQuests"] do
                                    safeServiceCall(EggService, "openEgg", eggName, 999)
