    Name = "Auto Buy All Fishing Upgrades",
    Description = "Buys every affordable fishing upgrade regardless of selection.",
    flagName = "AutoBuyAllFishingUpgrades",
    tag = "RCU_AutoBuyAllFishingUpgrades",

    Step = function()
        buyFishingUpgradesBatch(10)

        end
    end,
})

createIntervalToggle(Worlds, {
    Name = "Auto Buy Selected Space Upgrades",
    Description = "Only buys upgrades selected in the dropdown.",
    flagName = "AutoBuySelectedSpaceUpgrades",
    tag = "RCU_AutoBuySelectedSpaceUpgrades",
    delay = 4,
    Step = function()
        local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedWorldSpaceUpgrades"])
        if #selected == 0 then return end
        local _, nameMap = getSpaceUpgradeOptions()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        local upgrades = safeRequirePath(ReplicatedStorage, { "Shared", "List", "Space", "Upgrades" }, "Space.Upgrades") or {}
        for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
            local upgradeId = nameMap[display]
            local upData = upgrades[upgradeId]
            if upgradeId and upData and upData.upgrades then
                local currentLevel = data.spaceUpgrades and data.spaceUpgrades[upgradeId] or 0
                for i = currentLevel + 1, #upData.upgrades do
                    local cost = upData.upgrades[i].cost
                    local canAfford = false
                    if not cost then canAfford = true
                    elseif type(cost) == "number" then
                        local coinsItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, "spaceCoins")
                        local coins = coinsItem and coinsItem:getAmount() or 0
                        if coins >= cost then canAfford = true end
                    elseif type(cost) == "table" then
                        local costName = readCostName(cost)
                        local costAmt = readCostAmount(cost)
                        if costName and costAmt > 0 then
                            local have = getItemAmountByNameForAutoBuy(data, costName)
                            if have >= costAmt then canAfford = true end
                        end
                    end
                    if canAfford then
                        local result = safeServiceCall(UpgradeService, "upgradeSpace", upgradeId)
                        if result == "success" or result == true then
                            task.wait(0.15)
                            data = getData() or data
                        else break end
                    else break end
                end
            end
        end
    end,
})

        local _, map = getSmoothieOptions()
        local smoothieId = map[selected]
        local amount = math.max(tonumber(Library.Flags["SmoothieCraftAmount"]) or 1, 1)
        if not smoothieId then return end
        task.spawn(function()

                if i < amount then task.wait(1) end
            end
        end)
    end,
})

        task.spawn(function()

createIntervalToggle(Machines, {
    Name = "Auto Craft Magic Pot",
    flagName = "AutoCraftMagicPot",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCraftMagicPot",
    delay = 5,
    Step = function()
        local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedMagicPotItems"])
        if #selected == 0 then return end
        local _, map = getMagicPotOptions()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
            local info = map[display]
            if info and info.recipe then
                local recipe = info.recipe
                local maxCraft = math.huge
                if recipe.required then
                    for _, req in ipairs(recipe.required) do
                        local item = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, req.nm)
                        local amt = item and item:getAmount() or 0
                        local need = req.am or 1
                        maxCraft = math.min(maxCraft, math.floor(amt / need))
                    end
                end
                if recipe.requiredMastery and data.mastery and data.mastery < recipe.requiredMastery then
                    maxCraft = 0
                end
                if maxCraft and maxCraft > 0 and maxCraft < math.huge then
                    safeServiceCall(RewardService, "magicPot", info.id, maxCraft)
                    task.wait(1)
                end
            end
        end
    end,
})

        local wt = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedLumberjackWorkTime"], "1 Hour")

        end
        if status == "idle" or status == "ready_to_claim" then

        end
    end,

steampunkItemDropdown = Machines:createDropdown({
    Name = "Steampunk Items to Use",
    flagName = "SelectedSteampunkItems",
    List = {},
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Machines, {
    Name = "Auto Steampunk Machine",
    flagName = "AutoSteampunkMachine",
    tag = "RCU_AutoSteampunkMachine",
    delay = 5,
    Step = function()
        local selected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedSteampunkUpgrade"])
        if not selected then return end
        local _, upgradeMap = getSteampunkUpgradeOptions()
        local upgradeId = upgradeMap[selected]
        if not upgradeId or hasSteampunkBoost(upgradeId) then return end
        local items = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedSteampunkItems"])
        local _, itemMap = getSteampunkItemOptions(upgradeId)
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        local available = {}
        for _, display in ipairs(items) do
            local info = itemMap[display]
            if info then
                local item = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, info.name)
                if item and item:getAmount() >= info.amount then
                    table.insert(available, info)
                end
            end
        end
        if #available > 0 then
            local pick = available[math.random(#available)]
            safeServiceCall(RewardService, "steampunkMachine", upgradeId, pick.index)
        end
    end,
})

        local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedLunarForgeItems"])

        local _, map = getLunarForgeOptions()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
            local info = map[display]
            if info then
                local playerItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, info.item and info.item:getName() or "")
                local playerAmt = playerItem and playerItem:getAmount() or 0
                local need = info.requiredAmount or 1
                local maxCraft = math.floor(playerAmt / need)
                if maxCraft > 0 then
                    safeServiceCall(RewardService, "lunarForge", info.id, maxCraft)
                    task.wait(1)
                end
            end
        end
    end,
})

        local selected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedSpaceCrate"])
        if not selected then return end
        local _, map = getSpaceCrateOptions()
        local crate = map[selected]
        if not crate then return end
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        local coinsItem = itemUtils.getItemFromName and itemUtils.getItemFromName(data, "spaceCoins")
        local coins = coinsItem and coinsItem:getAmount() or 0
        if coins >= crate.price then
            safeServiceCall(BackpackService, "openCrate", crate.id)
        end
    end,

Machines:createLabel({
    Name = "Relic Upgrades",
    Special = true,
})
Machines:createDropdown({
    Name = "Select Relics to Upgrade",
    flagName = "SelectedRelics",
    List = getRelicOptions(),
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Machines, {
    Name = "Auto Craft Relics",
    flagName = "AutoCraftRelics",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCraftRelics",
    delay = 5,
    Step = function()
        local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedRelics"])
        if #selected == 0 then return end
        local _, map = getRelicOptions()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        for _, display in ipairs(selected) do
            local info = map[display]
            if info and info.data and info.data.craftingTiers then
                for tierIdx, tier in ipairs(info.data.craftingTiers) do
                    local required = tier.required
                    if required then
                        local playerAmt = 0
                        if data.inventory then
                            for _, cat in pairs(data.inventory) do
                                if type(cat) == "table" then
                                    for _, item in pairs(cat) do
                                        if type(item) == "table" and item.nm == required then
                                            playerAmt = playerAmt + (item.am or 1)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        local need = tier.requiredAmount or 1
                        local maxCraft = math.floor(playerAmt / need)
                        if maxCraft > 0 then
                            safeServiceCall(BackpackService, "upgradeRelic", info.id, tierIdx, maxCraft)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end,
})

    Name = "Falling Stars Event",

        if os.time() - last >= 79200 then
            safeServiceCall(FallingStarsService, "activateFallingStarsEvent")
        end
    end,
})

-- ===== COCONUTS / BASKET =====
Events:createLabel({
    Name = "Coconuts / Basket",
    Special = true,
})

createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Equip Basket",
    flagName = "AutoEquipBasket",
    tag = "RCU_AutoEquipBasket",
    delay = 3,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local data = getData()
            if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.summer2026 then return end
            local basketField = data.isBasketEquipped or data.basketEquipped
            if basketField then return end
            local itemId = findSummerItemByCategory("basket")
            if itemId then
                safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", itemId)
            end
        end)
    end,
})

createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Collect Coconuts",
    flagName = "AutoCollectCoconuts",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCollectCoconuts",
    delay = 0.5,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local data = getData()
            if not data or not data.palmTrees then return end
            if not data.isBasketEquipped then return end
            for palmTreeId, palmData in pairs(data.palmTrees) do
                local ptId = tonumber(palmTreeId)
                if not ptId then continue end
                if type(palmData.coconuts) ~= "table" then continue end
                for coconutId in pairs(palmData.coconuts) do
                    if type(coconutId) ~= "string" then continue end
                    local ok = safeServiceCall(SummerService, "collectCocounut", ptId, coconutId)
                    if ok then return end
                end
            end
        end)
    end,
})

crackerDropdown = Events:createDropdown({
    Name = "Crackers to Use",
    flagName = "SelectedSummerCrackers",
    List = getSummerCrackerOptions(),
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Crack Selected Coconuts",
    flagName = "AutoCrackCoconuts",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCrackCoconuts",
    delay = 1,
    Step = function()
        local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedSummerCrackers"])
        local useAll = #selected == 0
        local crackerDefs = getSummerModule("CoconutCracker")
        if crackerDefs then
            for crackerId in pairs(crackerDefs) do
                local label = tostring(crackerId)
                if useAll or hasValue(selected, label) or hasValue(selected, tostring(crackerDefs[crackerId].name or "") ) then
                    if safeServiceCall(SummerService, "useCoconutCracker", crackerId, 1) then return end
                end
            end
        else
            for crackerId = 1, 50 do
                if useAll or hasValue(selected, "Cracker " .. crackerId) then
                    if not safeServiceCall(SummerService, "useCoconutCracker", crackerId, 1) then break end
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end
        end
    end,
})
Events:createButton({
    Name = "Refresh Cracker List",
    Callback = function()
        crackerDropdown:updateList(getSummerCrackerOptions())
    end,
})

        safeServiceCall(SummerService, "upgradeBasket")
    end,

Events:createLabel({
    Name = "Palm Tree Upgrades",
    Special = true,
})

palmUpgradeDropdown = Events:createDropdown({
    Name = "Palm Upgrades to Buy",
    flagName = "SelectedPalmUpgrades",
    List = getSummerPalmUpgradeOptions(),
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Buy Selected Palm Upgrades",
    flagName = "AutoBuyPalmUpgrades",
    tag = "RCU_AutoBuyPalmUpgrades",
    delay = 1.5,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedPalmUpgrades"])
            local useAll = #selected == 0
            local upgradeDefs = getSummerModule("PalmUpgrades")
            if upgradeDefs then
                for upgradeName in pairs(upgradeDefs) do
                    local display = humanizeToken(upgradeName)
                    if useAll or hasValue(selected, upgradeName) or hasValue(selected, display) then
                        safeServiceCall(SummerService, "buyPalmUpgrade", upgradeName)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end
                return
            end
            local data = getData()
            if data and data.palmUpgrades then
                for upgradeName in pairs(data.palmUpgrades) do
                    if useAll or hasValue(selected, upgradeName) or hasValue(selected, humanizeToken(upgradeName)) then
                        safeServiceCall(SummerService, "buyPalmUpgrade", upgradeName)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end
                return
            end
            tryServiceCallUntilFail(SummerService, "buyPalmUpgrade", 1, 0.1)
        end)
    end,
})
Events:createButton({
    Name = "Refresh Palm Upgrades",
    Callback = function()
        palmUpgradeDropdown:updateList(getSummerPalmUpgradeOptions())
    end,
})

    Name = "Items to Evolve",
    flagName = "SelectedEvolutionItems",
    List = getSummerEvolutionOptions(),
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Evolve Selected Items",
    flagName = "AutoEvolutionMachine",
    tag = "RCU_AutoEvolutionMachine",
    delay = 1,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedEvolutionItems"])
            local useAll = #selected == 0
            local data = getData()
            if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.summer2026 then return end
            local ids = {}
            for idx, raw in pairs(data.inventory.summer2026) do
                if type(raw) ~= "table" then continue end
                local numId = tonumber(idx)
                if not numId then continue end
                if useAll or hasValue(selected, raw.nm) or hasValue(selected, raw.name) or hasValue(selected, humanizeToken(raw.nm or "")) then
                    table.insert(ids, numId)
                end
            end
            if #ids > 0 then
                safeServiceCall(SummerService, "evolve", ids, true, 999)
            end
        end)
    end,
})
Events:createButton({
    Name = "Refresh Evolution Items",
    Callback = function()
        evolutionDropdown:updateList(getSummerEvolutionOptions())
    end,
})

tikiAltarDropdown = Events:createDropdown({
    Name = "Tiki Altar Recipes to Craft",
    flagName = "SelectedTikiAltarRecipes",
    List = getSummerTikiAltarOptions(),
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Events, {
    Name = "Auto Craft Selected Tiki Altar Recipes",
    flagName = "AutoCraftTikiAltar",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCraftTikiAltar",
    delay = 2,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedTikiAltarRecipes"])
            local useAll = #selected == 0
            local defs = getSummerModule("TikiAltar")
            if not defs then return end
            for i, recipe in ipairs(defs) do
                local label
                if recipe.required and #recipe.required > 0 then
                    local ok, name = pcall(function() return tostring(recipe.required[1]:getRealName()) end)
                    if ok and name and name ~= "" then label = name end
                end
                if not label then label = "Recipe " .. i end
                if useAll or hasValue(selected, label) then
                    local ok = safeServiceCall(SummerService, "useTikiAltar", i, 1)
                    if not ok then break end
                    task.wait(0.2)
                end
            end
        end)
    end,
})
Events:createButton({
    Name = "Refresh Tiki Altar List",
    Callback = function()
        tikiAltarDropdown:updateList(getSummerTikiAltarOptions())
    end,
})

    tag = "RCU_AutoClaimCoconutIslandChest",

        pcall(function()
            local data = getData()

            if data.claimedCoconutIslandChest then
                local currentHour = math.floor(os.time() / 3600)
                if hasValue(data.claimedCoconutIslandChest, currentHour) then
                    return
                end
            end
            safeServiceCall(CoconutIslandService, "claimCoconutIslandChest")
        end)
    end,
})

Events:createLabel({
    Name = "Season Quest Config",
    Special = true,
})

do
    local eggOpts, displayMap = getSeasonEggList()
    if #eggOpts > 0 then
        local defaultEgg = eggOpts[1]
        SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg = displayMap[defaultEgg] or defaultEgg:match("^(.-) %-") or defaultEgg
        SeasonQuestState.selectedMythicalEternalEgg = SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg

        Events:createDropdown({
            Name = "Open Egg Quest",
            flagName = "SeasonQuestEgg",
            List = eggOpts,
            Flag = { defaultEgg },
            Callback = function(value)
                local v = type(value) == "table" and value[1] or value
                SeasonQuestState.selectedQuestEgg = resolveBestEgg(v, eggOpts, displayMap) or v
            end,
        })

        Events:createDropdown({
            Name = "Open Egg Mythical/Eternal",
            flagName = "SeasonMythicalEgg",
            List = eggOpts,
            Flag = { defaultEgg },
            Callback = function(value)
                local v = type(value) == "table" and value[1] or value
                SeasonQuestState.selectedMythicalEternalEgg = resolveBestEgg(v, eggOpts, displayMap) or v
            end,
        })
    end

    local auraOpts = getAuraDiceList()
    if #auraOpts > 0 then
        Events:createDropdown({
            Name = "Select Aura Dice",
            flagName = "SeasonAuraDice",
            multi = true,
            List = auraOpts,
            Flag = { "Aura Dice" },
            Callback = function(value)
                SeasonQuestState.selectedAuraDice = type(value) == "table" and value or {}
            end,
        })
    end

    local questOpts = getAllSeasonQuests()
    if #questOpts > 0 then
        Events:createDropdown({
            Name = "Select Quests (leave empty for all)",
            flagName = "SeasonQuestsSelection",
            multi = true,
            List = questOpts,
            Flag = {},
            Callback = function(value)
                local raw = type(value) == "table" and value or {}
                local types = {}
                for qName, isSel in pairs(raw) do
                    if isSel then
                        local qt = qName:match("%] (.+)$")
                        if qt then table.insert(types, qt) end
                    end
                end
                SeasonQuestState.selectedQuests = types
            end,
        })

        Events:createButton({
            Name = "Select All Quests",
            Callback = function()
                local all = {}
                for _, qn in ipairs(questOpts) do all[qn] = true end
                if Library.Flags["SeasonQuestsSelection"] ~= nil then
                    Library.Flags["SeasonQuestsSelection"] = all
                end
                local types = {}
                for qName in pairs(all) do
                    local qt = qName:match("%] (.+)$")
                    if qt then table.insert(types, qt) end
                end
                SeasonQuestState.selectedQuests = types
            end,
        })
    end
end

createIntervalToggle(Rewards, {
    Name = "Auto Play Ancient Rewards Minigame",
    flagName = "AutoPlayAncientRewards",
    tag = "RCU_AutoPlayAncientRewards",
    delay = 0.25,
    Step = function()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        local hasTickets = false
        if data.inventory and data.inventory.exclusive then
            for _, item in pairs(data.inventory.exclusive) do
                if item.nm == "ancientTicket" and (item.am or 1) > 0 then
                    hasTickets = true
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        if hasTickets then
            local result = safeServiceCall(RewardService, "claimAncientReward")
            if result ~= "success" then
                task.wait(1)
            end
        end
    end,
})

    Name = "Auto Use",
    Special = true,
})
fruitDropdown = Inventory:createDropdown({
    Name = "Select Fruits to Use",
    flagName = "SelectedFruits",
    List = {},
    Flag = {},
    multi = true,
    Callback = function() end,
})
Inventory:createButton({
    Name = "Refresh Fruit List",
    Callback = function()
        local opts, seen = {}, {}
        local data = getData()
        if data and data.inventory and data.inventory.fruit then
            for id, raw in pairs(data.inventory.fruit) do
                local name = type(raw) == "table" and (raw.nm or raw.name) or nil
                if not name then name = id:match("^[^_]+") or id end
                if not seen[name] then
                    seen[name] = true
                    table.insert(opts, name)
                end
            end
        end
        table.sort(opts)
        fruitDropdown:updateList(opts)
    end,
})
local autoUseFruitsThread = nil
Inventory:createToggle({
    Name = "Auto Use Fruits",
    flagName = "AutoUseFruits",
    Flag = false,
    Callback = function(enabled)
        if not enabled and autoUseFruitsThread then task.cancel(autoUseFruitsThread); autoUseFruitsThread = nil end
        if enabled then
            autoUseFruitsThread = task.spawn(function()
                while Library.Flags["AutoUseFruits"] do
                    local data = getData()
                    if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.fruit then task.wait(3); continue end
                    local selected = readSelectedDropdownValues(Library.Flags["SelectedFruits"])
                    local used = 0
                    for id, item in pairs(data.inventory.fruit) do
                        if used >= 12 then break end
                        local itemName = type(item) == "table" and (item.nm or item.name) or tostring(id)
                        if #selected == 0 or tableFind(selected, itemName) then
                            local amt = type(item) == "table" and (item.am or item.amount or 1) or 1
                            if amt > 0 then
                                local result = safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", id, { use = 1 })
                                if result == "success" or result == true then
                                    used = used + 1
                                    task.wait(0.1)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(3)
                end
                autoUseFruitsThread = nil
            end)
        end
    end,
})

createIntervalToggle(Inventory, {
    Name = "Auto Use All Fruits",
    flagName = "AutoUseAllFruits",
    tag = "RCU_AutoUseAllFruits",
    delay = 3,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local data = getData()
            if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.fruit then return end
            local used = 0
            for id, item in pairs(data.inventory.fruit) do
                if used >= 25 then break end
                local amt = type(item) == "table" and (item.am or item.amount or 1) or 1
                if amt > 0 then
                    local result = safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", id, { use = 1 })
                    if result == "success" or result == true then
                        used = used + 1
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end
            end
        end)
    end,
})

createIntervalToggle(Inventory, {
    Name = "Auto Use All Aura Dice",
    flagName = "AutoUseAllAuraDice",
    tag = "RCU_AutoUseAllAuraDice",
    delay = 1,
    Step = function()
        pcall(function()
            local data = getData()
            if not data or not data.inventory or not data.inventory.auraDice then return end
            for id, _ in pairs(data.inventory.auraDice) do
                local result = safeServiceCall(InventoryService, "useItem", id, { use = 1 })
                if result == "success" or result == true then
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end
        end)
    end,
})

createIntervalToggle(Inventory, {
    Name = "Auto Craft Selected Ring",
    flagName = "AutoCraftSelectedRing",
    tag = "RCU_AutoCraftSelectedRing",
    delay = 8,
    Step = function()
        local selected = getFirstSelectedDropdownValue(Library.Flags["SelectedRing"])
        if not selected then return end
        local _, map = getRingOptions()
        local ringId = map[selected]
        if ringId then
            safeServiceCall(RingService, "craftRing", ringId, 1)
        end
    end,
})

    Callback = function()

            notify("Mount Equipped", "Spawned " .. tostring(selected) .. " locally.", "info")

    end,

    flagName = "DisableParticles",
    Flag = false,
    Callback = function(enabled)
        Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag("RCU_DisableParticles")
        if not enabled then return end
        interval("RCU_DisableParticles", "DisableParticles", 5, function()
            disableParticleEffects(Workspace)
        end)
    end,
})
Settings:createToggle({
    Name = "Low Quality Terrain",
    flagName = "LowQualityTerrain",
    Flag = false,
    Callback = function(enabled)
        pcall(function()
            local terrain = Workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain")
            if not terrain then return end
            terrain.Decoration = not enabled
        end)
    end,
})
Settings:createToggle({
    Name = "Remove Textures and Decals",
    flagName = "DisableTextures",
    Flag = false,
    Callback = function(enabled)
        Library:CleanupConnectionsByTag("RCU_DisableTextures")
        if enabled then
            interval("RCU_DisableTextures", "DisableTextures", 10, function()
                stripTextures(Workspace)
            end)
        end
    end,
})
Settings:createSlider({
    Name = "FPS Cap",
    Description = "0 = unlimited",
    flagName = "FPSCap",
    value = 60,
    minValue = 0,
    maxValue = 240,
    Callback = function(value)
        pcall(function()
            if setfpscap then setfpscap(value == 0 and math.huge or value) end
        end)
    end,
})
Settings:createSlider({
    Name = "Render Distance",
    flagName = "RenderDistance",
    value = 2500,
    minValue = 100,
    maxValue = 10000,
    Callback = function(value)
        pcall(function()
            client.ReplicationFocus = nil
            settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = Enum.QualityLevel.Level01
            LightingService.FogEnd = value
        end)
    end,
})

Rejoin = Setup:CreateSection("🔄 Rejoin")
Rejoin:createLabel({
    Name = "Auto Rejoin",
    Special = true,
})
Rejoin:createInputBox({
    Name = "Public Rejoin Delay (seconds)",
    flagName = "PublicRejoinDelay",
    Flag = 3600,
    Callback = function() end,
})
createIntervalToggle(Rejoin, {
    Name = "Auto Rejoin Public Server",
    flagName = "AutoRejoinPublic",
    tag = "RCU_AutoRejoinPublic",
    delay = 1,
    Step = function()
        local last = RejoinRuntimeState.lastPublicRejoinAt or 0
        local waitTime = tonumber(Library.Flags["PublicRejoinDelay"]) or 3600
        if os.clock() - last < waitTime then return end
        RejoinRuntimeState.lastPublicRejoinAt = os.clock()
        rejoinPublicServer()
    end,
})

Webhooks:createButton({
    Name = "Send Closest Egg Info Webhook",
    Callback = function()
        local fields, title = buildClosestEggInfoFields()
        if sendRCUWebhook("rcu_egg_info", title, fields, {
            Description = "Closest visible egg, global/special spawn metadata, model attributes, cost, and hatchable pet table.",
        }, false) then
            notify("Webhook Sent", "Closest egg info sent.", "info")
        else
            notify("Webhook Not Sent", "Paste a Discord webhook URL first.", "warning")
        end
    end,
})

DevTools = Setup:CreateSection("🛠️ Developer Tools")
DevTools:createLabel({
    Name = "Developer Tools",
    Special = true,
})
DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Print RCU Data Keys",
    Callback = function()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then
            warn("[RCU] No DataController.data yet")
            return
        end
        print("======== RCU DATA KEYS ========")
        for key, value in pairs(data) do
            print(key, typeof(value), type(value) == "table" and countTable(value) or value)
        end
        print("================================")
    end,
})

DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Print Visible Tree/Ore Counts",
    Callback = function()
        print("[RCU] Trees:", #CollectionService:GetTagged("Tree"))
        print("[RCU] Ores:", #CollectionService:GetTagged("Ore"))
        print("[RCU] AFK Ores:", #CollectionService:GetTagged("AfkOre"))
        print("[RCU] Ore Rooms:", table.concat(getOreRooms(), ", "))
    end,
})

DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Print Services Loaded",
    Callback = function()
        local loaded = {
            ClickService = ClickService ~= nil,
            EggService = EggService ~= nil,
            RebirthService = RebirthService ~= nil,
            TreeService = TreeService ~= nil,
            OreService = OreService ~= nil,
            DungeonService = DungeonService ~= nil,
            RewardService = RewardService ~= nil,
            UpgradeService = UpgradeService ~= nil,
            HiveService = HiveService ~= nil,
            TotemService = TotemService ~= nil,
            DataController = DataController ~= nil,
            TreeController = TreeController ~= nil,
            OreController = OreController ~= nil,
            DungeonController = DungeonController ~= nil,
            TotemController = TotemController ~= nil,
        }
        prettyPrint(loaded)
    end,
})

DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Print Session Stats",
    Callback = function()
        print("[RCU Session]", RCUSessionStats)
        notify("Session Stats", "Printed to console (F9).", "info")
    end,
})
DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Print Player Currencies",
    Callback = function()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        print("clicks", getCurrency(data, "clicks"))
        print("gems", getCurrency(data, "gems"))
        print("rebirths", data.rebirths)
    end,
})
DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Dump Upgrade Levels",
    Callback = function()
        local data = getData()
        if not data or not data.upgrades then return end
        prettyPrint(data.upgrades)
    end,
})
DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Dump Hive Data",
    Callback = function()
        local data = getData()
        if not data then return end
        print("honeyToCollect", data.honeyToCollect)
        print("equippedBees", data.equippedBees)
        print("hiveUpgrades", data.hiveUpgrades)
    end,
})
DevTools:createButton({
    Name = "Dump Farm Ownership",
    Callback = function()
        prettyPrint(getData() and getData().farms or {})
    end,
})
